Current Commentary

How to Face the Year 1933

Time passes. We approach the beginning of 1933. What state will China be in during 1933? What changes will occur? This is a question not only for the Chinese people under imperialist aggression, who are racking their brains seeking an answer, but also for informed people worldwide who are concerned. Since 1929, the global economic crisis has intensified daily, surging relentlessly. The root cause of the crisis is the overproduction of all commodities. The result of overproduction is a general decline in prices. The relentless decline in prices eventually leads to revenue from sales being insufficient to cover production costs, forcing producers to lay off workers and reduce production. The laying off of workers had already begun among the great powers, who advocated industrial rationalization, adopting new machinery and improving factory organization. Overproduction spread and became particularly severe, leading to serious unemployment. As the number of unemployed increased, general purchasing power sharply declined, further exacerbating overproduction. Overproduction and unemployment became mutually causative, creating a seemingly intractable situation.

In recent years, disputes in the international community, such as the general issues of tariff truce, disarmament, and war debts, as well as specific issues like the Sino-Japanese problem, are all inevitable products of overproduction and economic crisis. Due to domestic overproduction, the great powers had no choice but to passively raise tariff barriers to prevent the import of products from other countries and actively expand their military capabilities to seize colonies. Some dreamers then tried to use their eloquent tongues to mediate and avert disaster. This is the reason for the tariff truce and disarmament conferences. The war debt problem became so serious because, after the tariff barriers were raised, Germany could no longer use its surplus goods to pay reparations. Paying reparations in cash was impossible, leading to the open declaration of inability to continue payments. European countries, in turn, argued for suspending war debt payments to the United States due to the suspension of German reparations. Under capitalism, a nation's strength relies on the efforts and plunder of the bourgeoisie, and national fiscal revenue depends on sharing the spoils of that plunder. After the economic crisis, trade sharply declined and industries withered. The tax revenue, income tax, business tax, etc., which were formerly the main sources of national revenue, suffered significant blows. This led even the United States, a nation generally perceived as a land of gold, to be unable to balance its budget and experience such severe fiscal depletion. How could it generously allow the suspension of these enormous war debts? This is why the war debt issue has been repeatedly disputed without resolution. Moreover, the Sino-Japanese problem is an inevitable result of the expansion of surplus goods by Japanese imperialism. I have previously provided a more detailed discussion in my article "Future Actions of Japanese Imperialism towards China." It is clear that all international developments are driven by economic factors.

The theory of cycles of prosperity and decline is not only cherished by our ancient philosophers, but also regarded as sound reasoning by Western economists, as exemplified by the so-called "law of economic cycles." We do not intend to fundamentally deny the law of economic cycles, but we must revise it. Since the beginning of human history, no system has remained unchanged. The brilliant culture is achieved through metabolism. Therefore, the economic cycle is to a social system what the passage of time is to human life. Each cycle changes the content of life, from infancy to youth, from youth to adulthood, from adulthood to old age, from old age to sickness, and from sickness to death. Meanwhile, the young generation rises. The continuation of mankind remains the same, while racial improvement progresses daily. The necessity of system change is like the necessity of experiencing birth, aging, sickness, and death in human life. Therefore, the so-called economic cycle is a revolving lantern-like cycle, but also a spiral-like advance. The silkworm undergoes three sleeps and gradually transforms. The meaning of each of the three sleeps is different. The phrase "time urges people to grow old" applies to the economic cycle, which continues to urge the current system from infancy to prosperity, and from prosperity to decline. We can see from the history of human society and the general course of human life that the current system must meet its end under some crisis.

Su Bingwen Compiles Report on Japanese Atrocities, to be Sent to Geneva

=Stalin Invites Su's Troops to Work=

=Su Bingwen Politely Declines via Telegram=

(Beiping) Su Bingwen's secretary, He Shengda, telegraphed from Vladivostok on the 4th, stating that Su had telegraphed Yan Huiqing, our representative in Geneva, saying that his trip to Geneva might not materialize and asking if the report on Japanese atrocities could be compiled into a book and sent to Geneva. Yan replied approvingly. The report is now being compiled and will be completed by the 8th and sent to Geneva. Stalin, the People's Commissar of the Soviet Union, telegraphed Su Bingwen from Moscow, inviting his troops to participate in labor. Su replied with a telegram, politely declining, saying that he would consider it later. Currently, Su's troops, though living hard lives daily, are in high spirits, performing callisthenics three times a day and studying academic subjects for several hours (starting from the 7th).

(Beiping) Su Bingwen has recently shown great interest in Vladivostok's industries, frequently visiting factories and farms. Wang Zaisi, secretary of the Chinese delegation to the Sino-Soviet Conference, recently came from Moscow with a Soviet government representative to Vladivostok to meet with Su and discuss important matters. They will return to Moscow tomorrow or the day after. Furthermore, Su was greatly angered by the news of the fall of Yuguan and plans to return to China soon with Ma Zhanshan, Xie Ke, and Zhang Dianjiu to participate in the war of resistance against Japan. All the soldiers are indignant at Japan's unprovoked invasion of Yuguan and are eager to return to their homeland to serve on the battlefield and repay their country (special dispatch on the 7th).

Russian Newspaper Comments on the Yuguan Incident

Japanese Troops Invading Yuguan Only a Prelude to Attacking Jehol

Conflict Between Imperialist Powers Ultimately Inevitable

(Moscow) Foreign news agencies reported that the Soviet government's bulletin, "Izvestia," had published an article on January 4th regarding the Japanese invasion of Shanhaiguan, but this was inaccurate. The newspaper only published an editorial today expressing its views on the serious situation in North China. According to the newspaper, after seizing Shanhaiguan, the Japanese troops are in an advantageous position, able to reach Tianjin directly without difficulty and arrive in Beiping within three hours. The occupation of Shanhaiguan is, in fact, the beginning of a long-expected attack on Jehol. "Pravda" pointed out that after discussing the Lytton Report, the League of Nations had shelved the attempt to resolve the Manchurian problem, granting Japan the opportunity to take further military action. At the same time, Japanese imperialism deeply understands that the United States, during this period of political transition, will inevitably relax its policy on the Far East issue. Regarding the question of whether the attack on Shanhaiguan is the beginning of an invasion of North China and Jehol, the newspaper said that the Japanese troops attacking Zhang Xueliang's and Tang Yulin's troops have not yet fully decided on this step. The Japanese are well aware that invading North China and Jehol is not simply a military action. This move could cause the Shanghai incident of last year to repeat itself, inevitably increase international disputes, and further stimulate China's national struggle. Regarding the anti-Japanese forces, the newspaper pointed out that the volunteer armies in Jehol and the remaining volunteer forces in North and South Manchuria are still active. However, it ultimately stated that Japanese imperialism is preparing to invade Jehol and North China and is preparing intensely. Although it has not yet entered the "main event," Japanese imperialism believes that the international situation is favorable to its new adventures. "Red Star," the organ of the Red Army, said that foreign observers believe that the Japanese invasion of Shanhaiguan is another step in realizing the "Tanaka Plan," which is not without significance. Although the plan has been denied by the Japanese, Japan's policy towards China proves its existence. The newspaper pointed out that the hypocritical attitude of the League of Nations and France's open approval of Japanese actions are all beneficial to Japan, and Japan also knows that the current paralysis of American diplomacy will not take strict measures to prevent its actions against Jehol. However, it finally stated that Japan has infringed upon the vital interests of the United States, Britain, and other imperialist powers. Therefore, although no open conflict has occurred at present, there will inevitably be a time of great explosion in the future (TASS dispatch on the 6th).

Bao Wenwei Arrives in Nanjing Yesterday

Reports on the Yuguan Incident

Requests Instructions on How to Respond

(Nanjing) Zhang Xueliang's representative, Bao Wenwei, arrived in Nanjing on orders to report everything to the Central Government and Chairman Chiang. He arrived in Nanjing at 9:30 this morning. He stated that the Japanese army's invasion of Yuguan was a deliberate act of aggression, attempting to disturb Jehol and the Beiping-Tianjin area. He Shi'an's regiment valiantly resisted at Yuguan, resulting in several hundred Japanese casualties. Our own casualties were also significant, details of which have already been reported. As of the evening of the 5th when he left Beiping, Brigade Commander He Zhuguo was still supervising the defense at the front lines, and there were no further intense clashes. The Qinhuangdao area was also still calm. Various rumors circulating were inaccurate. Although the Jehol border was tense, Chairman Tang was prepared to defend the territory to the death and had made ample preparations. If the Japanese invade, we will have no choice but to resist and defend our territory. Tianjin was still safe. Chairman Yu, who had been inspecting various counties, had also rushed back to oversee the situation. The generals in North China were all deeply indignant and eagerly requested to fight the enemy. However, resistance against Japan requires an overall plan. My trip to Nanjing is to report to the Central Government and Chairman Chiang on the Japanese army's invasion of Yuguan and our army's resistance, and to request instructions on the overall response plan. I will be stationed in Nanjing for the near future to handle all related matters. Reports that Japan considers the invasion of Yuguan to be a local incident and intends to negotiate directly with Vice Chairman Zhang are absolutely inaccurate. This is purely Japanese propaganda aimed at easing international pressure. The Japanese are accustomed to using this tactic and it is not worth laughing at. I am scheduled to visit Chairman Chiang tonight to report on everything, and will report to various military organizations this afternoon (special dispatch on the 7th).

(Nanjing) Zhang Xueliang's representative, Bao Wenwei, arrived in Nanjing on the morning of the 7th and met with Chairman Chiang that evening to report on the details of the Japanese army's invasion of Yuguan and request instructions. He will return to Beiping soon to report back (Central News Agency dispatch on the 7th).

(Nanjing) Zhang Xueliang's representative, Bao Wenwei, told people upon his arrival in Nanjing that the claim that Zhang intended to resolve the Yuguan case locally with the Japanese was completely inaccurate. This is Japanese propaganda aimed at confusing the public. Zhang Xueliang, Tang Yulin, and the various generals in the North are all determined to resist the Japanese army's invasion and have made ample preparations for the defense of Jehol. He will remain in Nanjing for some time to handle matters in North China (China News Agency dispatch on the 7th).

He Chengjun and He Jian Both Send Telegrams Urging Zhang Xueliang

You uphold the Central Government's established policy, implement the initial goal of resisting the enemy, and work hard with dedication. Your perseverance and sincerity are deeply admired. My troops are stationed in Qinzhong, driving out the "dogs and rats" like the sun advances relentlessly. I pledge to use the elite troops of Shaanxi and Hubei as your rearguard, so that we can recover the fields of Wenyang and wipe away the shame of Kuaiji. Peace and Security in Beiping Not a Concern

(Beiping) Zhou Dawen said that there is absolutely no problem with the peace and security of Beiping. Military police and constables are working overtime all night, patrolling. The current rumors are created by traitors and are not credible (special dispatch on the 7th).

(Beiping) Bao Yulin said that since the fall of Yuguan, numerous rumors have been circulating in Beiping and Tianjin. I am leading the city's police to step up patrols to protect the lives and property of the 1.5 million people of Beiping. Do not listen to rumors (special dispatch on the 7th).

(Beiping) After the Yuguan incident occurred, the Beiping authorities paid close attention to maintaining peace and security. Some rice and flour merchants took the opportunity to raise grain prices, with a bag of flour increasing by 30 cents and a bag of rice increasing by 3 yuan. The livelihood of the common people has been greatly affected. The municipal authorities will take measures to crack down on this (special dispatch on the 7th).

(Beiping) Zheng Guilin's volunteer army, numbering over 1,000, attacked Qiansuo on the night of the 6th, engaging in fierce fighting with the Japanese army. At around 2:00 AM this morning, Zheng's forces occupied Gaoling, five li from Qiansuo, destroying many Japanese supplies and capturing countless guns and ammunition. The Japanese rushed to dispatch troops from the attacking Yuguan force to provide reinforcements. Fierce fighting is still ongoing. At the same time, Zhang Guoxiang's 40th Route volunteer army attacked Xinmin, engaging in extremely fierce fighting. The pseudo-Fengshan Railway has completely suspended operations due to military transport (special dispatch on the 7th).

(Harbin) According to Japanese sources, Japanese troops led by the regimental commander of the Eastern Section of the Chinese Eastern Railway occupied Lishuzhuang last night. The area is not far from the Russian border. Troops led by Hito are currently advancing towards Mishan in order to eliminate Li Du's volunteer army. Japanese sources also said that the commander of the Chinese garrison in Suifenhe surrendered with his troops, without war. They have been disarmed by the Japanese army. The town was not damaged (Reuters dispatch on the 7th).

Cai Tingkai Takes Office as Pacification Director

Cai Issues Inaugural Telegram…

Use the Full Strength of the Entire Nation and People

Fight for Final Survival at This Moment

(Fuzhou) Cai Tingkai took office as Pacification Director on the 6th (special dispatch on the 7th).

(Fuzhou) Cai Tingkai issued a telegram on the 6th: To All Newspapers, In the case of the National Government's Appointment Order No. 66, it is stated, "Special appointment of Cai Tingkai as Director of the Pacification Commissioner's Office in Fujian, etc." Upon receiving the order, Tingkai is filled with trepidation. Reflecting on the national crisis, which has lasted for over a year, the lost territory of over two million square li in the Northeast has not been recovered, and the wounds from the month-long Battle of Shanghai have not healed. Our army reluctantly withdrew and moved to Fujian, originally intending to thoroughly replenish and await the decision of the central government. Since arriving in Fujian, the entire army has been on standby, ready to fight. Though we are in a remote area, our thoughts are with the borderlands. Recently, Yuguan fell, and Beiping and Tianjin are in imminent danger. North of the Yellow River will soon be lost to us. The volunteer armies outside the pass eat the wind and sleep in the snow, and their calls for help go unanswered. If the volunteer armies are exhausted, the pseudo-regime will gain momentum, and the Japanese will further increase their pretexts. Tingkai is a soldier, dedicated to serving the country, mindful of the duty to risk his life in danger and grieved by the impending doom of the nation. Looking north to Pan and Liao, I cannot sleep or eat. Now, I have received the decree and been entrusted with the defense of a vast territory. I have declined but to no avail and must reluctantly undertake this arduous task. I respectfully took office on January 6th, complying with the order and assuming my duties at the office. While striving to fulfill my local responsibilities, I dare not forget my determination to fight. I hope that all officials of our central government will unite in spirit, eliminate divisions, resolve internal disputes, and concentrate the nation's strength and talent. A national defense and military plan must be established as soon as possible to strengthen the central government and jointly address the crisis. We must use the full strength of the entire nation and people to fight for final survival at this moment. This is a critical juncture that allows no懈怠. Though I am foolish and ignorant, I humbly wish to lead the way, serving the country with all my might. Even if I have to wield the whip and carry the halberd, I will not refuse the labor. I am willing to wrap my body in horsehide and fulfill my long-cherished ambition. In addition to submitting this report, I am sending this telegram to express my thoughts and await your instructions. Cai Tingkai bows. (special dispatch on the 7th).

Japan Actively Prepares for War

=Will Shift National Forces to Northeast China, Striving for Scientific Modernization of Armaments=

=Improve Current Conscription System, Intensify Training of Junior Officers=

=Mobilize Young Men and Women, Organize Military Training Centers=

=Military Headquarters Directly Guiding Practical Exercises=

Reuters, Tokyo, 6th - The Ministry of the Army has released an article explaining the reasons for its troop increase in Manchuria and for making several important reforms to the army's organization, structure, training, and equipment. While the article doesn't discuss the extent of the troop increase in Manchuria, according to a spokesperson from the Ministry of the Army to a Reuters reporter, Manchuria currently has 40,000 soldiers, but this number will increase to 60,000 or 65,000 within the next two years. The increase will be in the number of people in the main force, not the number of troops. However, the number of special small detachments must also increase. The current four and a half divisions stationed in Manchuria (namely, the 8th, 10th, 14th, and 2nd divisions, as well as a portion of the 7th division, and the 1st and 4th Cavalry Brigades) are all peacetime forces. The peacetime troop strength of a division stationed in Manchuria is less than that of a division within Japan. When a division is sent to Manchuria, a portion of that division is always left in Japan for training new recruits and other important tasks. According to the currently announced plan, this system will be changed in the future, that is, the troop strength of the divisions stationed in Manchuria will be increased, and the number of people left in the country as trainers will be reduced. It is said that the independent railway protection unit, which is a permanent military force in Manchuria and has wartime troop strength, may also need to be increased from the current six battalions to twelve battalions. The tank units, heavy artillery units, railway units, and transportation units must also be greatly expanded so that they can perform their duties of maintaining peace and order in a vast and remote area. While increasing troops in Manchuria, the army is also reducing or reorganizing troops within Japan proper. According to the latter part of the Ministry of the Army's announcement, the proposal to increase troops in Manchuria is in accordance with the Japanese-Manchurian agreement to maintain peace and order in Manchuria. The troop increase in Manchuria is only part of the army's program. In addition, it is necessary to implement long-planned replenishment programs and revise the current conscription system. The so-called replenishment program includes increasing machinery, improving armaments, equipping everything, and special training in new weapons. Ordinary soldiers, reservists, and junior officers must also be given some special military education, totaling 100,000 people. The training includes the use of light and heavy machine guns, airplanes, tanks, automobiles, and radio, as well as protection against poison gas, observation of weather conditions, and surveying land. Special attention will also be given to the training of military dogs. The Japanese army has made rapid progress in this type of training in the past few years. The most important aspect of the required modifications to the conscription system is the recruitment and training of reserve officers, as the existing supply of officers will not be sufficient if war breaks out. In short, based on the Japanese Ministry of the Army's announcement, it can be seen that it has three main objectives: (1) Increase the troop strength in Manchuria and reorganize the entire army; (2) Increase the mechanization and mobility of the army; (3) Improve the existing conscription and training system.

China United Press, Tokyo - Since the incident at Yuguan, all sectors here have become very tense. The Ministry of the Army and the General Staff Headquarters have been holding secret military meetings for days. It is said that the scope of discussion includes not only concrete plans for the military invasion of Rehe, but also the full deployment of national military mobilization within the country. To give an example, the Ministry of the Army and the Ministry of Education have decided on a detailed and specific plan for the military training of young men and women students. According to the Ministry of the Army, the total number of young people across the country who should receive training is 2 million, of which 1 million have already received direct training. Among the young people employed in factories and businesses, currently (in Tokyo) there are 24 privately established training centers under the jurisdiction of the First Division, including Matsuya, Matsuzakaya, Shirokiya, Takashimaya, Dainippon Brewery, Tokyo Shikki, Dainippon Kogaku, and other munitions factories, with active duty officers assigned to directly guide them. Based on this policy, the Tokyo Automobile Industry Association, under the leadership of the Fascists, is actively recruiting young people, planning to establish youth training centers. The Kagawa Prefecture Barber Association has also established the "Seisan Private Youth Training Center," which is scheduled to expand to 3,000 people starting this spring, using two public holidays each month to begin practical training. Furthermore, according to investigations, the Ministry of the Army has designated the following schedule for practical exercises in various parts of the country this month: January 4th, joint exercises in Kurate District, Fukuoka Prefecture; 5th, joint exercises involving 17 townships in Hiroshima Prefecture's youth training and secondary schools; 8th, joint exercises involving 19 townships in Yamashi Prefecture's Kita-Koma District; 11th-12th, joint exercises involving 5 townships in Hiroshima Prefecture's Kita District, youth training, veterans, and middle school students; 11th, joint exercises involving the city of Hachioji and the Santo District in Tokyo; 13th, joint exercises involving Tagawa District, Fukuoka Prefecture; 17th, joint exercises involving three districts in Hiroshima Prefecture's Kita District; 21st, joint exercises involving Fukayasu District, Hiroshima Prefecture. Training for women is also becoming very active, with the organization of women's military control mobilization, women's youth groups, and troop dispatch comfort squads, all with extremely precise training. The principals of 61 private girls' schools in Tokyo have held meetings since last year. As a result, in addition to several sessions of carrying out live ammunition drills and wartime rescue training, they openly dispatched representatives to the military in a concrete negotiation on November 20th last year. It is heard that the Ministry of the Army has decided to mobilize young men and women across the country from this spring, April, to regularly practice military operations and educate them on military knowledge for use in invading China and attacking the Soviet Union.

Navy to Practice New Tactics

The Tokyo Asahi Shimbun reports that the Ministry of the Navy, in view of the increasingly tense international situation, has decided to bring forward the naval special grand exercises, which were originally held every four years. The exercises will be held this summer, centered on the Ogasawara Islands, encompassing a vast area of the tropical Pacific Ocean. Participating units will include the Combined Fleet, various naval districts, major ports, guard ships, reserve ships, etc., totaling 200 ships, plus air squadrons and ground units from various locations, encompassing the entire Japanese Navy. The exercises will focus on the latest tactics, such as dusk and dawn battles, night battles, night attacks, concentrated decisive battles, nighttime bombing and torpedo attacks by aircraft carrier fleets, strategic tracking and contact by submarines, and rapid close-quarters combat by the main fleet against enemy fleets using smoke screens.

No Change in Far East Policy After New US President Takes Office

Publication of Supplemental Agreement for the Control of Opium in the Far East

Effective Upon British Ratification

National News Agency, London, 7th - The Supplemental Agreement for the Strict Control of Smoking in the Far East, signed in Bangkok on November 27, 1931, by the United Kingdom, Ireland, France, India, Japan, the Netherlands, Portugal, and Siam, was published here today. However, the United Kingdom has not yet ratified it. The agreement stipulates that opium may only be sold in government-licensed and supervised shops. People under the age of twenty-one are not allowed to enter such shops or places where opium is smoked. Anyone who induces young people to smoke or sells opium to them will be severely punished. This agreement is an annex to the 1925 Geneva Opium Convention and will take effect after all signatory countries have ratified it.

Japan Massively Expands Military Preparations

=Enhance Military Preparedness to Cope with International Conflicts=

=Continue Secretly Transporting Troops to Invade North China=

Tokyo Correspondence - The Japanese Choshu clique has already blatantly invaded "Manchuria." However, it is very afraid of China rising up to fight. Many people believe that it is afraid of the great powers interfering, but in reality, the great powers have no power to interfere. In particular, the United States currently has no way to wage war in the Western Pacific, which is something that the Japanese Satsuma and Choshu cliques have recognized. While they are naturally wary of the great powers, especially of Red Russia, they only intend to further invade China. Looking at the budget recently released by their Ministry of Finance, the army's expenses alone amount to 447,883,000 Japanese yen, of which 114,645,000 Japanese yen is for military equipment improvement, and the expenses for invading the Northeast, including those of the army, navy, Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Ministry of Finance, and Ministry of Communications, total 186,330,000 Japanese yen. From the above figures, we know that there are two special facts being expressed: First, they are implementing their so-called military equipment improvement, and second, they are increasing troops in Manchuria.

Military Preparedness Improvement

The so-called improvement of military preparedness has two sources. One is in view of the international situation, where the military equipment of all army nations is very sophisticated, with balanced allocations of airplanes, tanks, and poison gas. The Soviet Union even has four mechanized divisions. The second is the use of new weapons. The training in Japan is not only lacking in elite personnel but also small in number. If they were to encounter a real war, the Japanese army would find it difficult to cope with the enemy. Therefore, Japan is actively working on improving its military preparedness. The main items for improvement are roughly as follows:

(1) Enhancing lower-level officers, increasing the number of officers and military school students (reportedly the first step is 100,000 people).

(2) To supplement the current shortage of junior lieutenants and lieutenants, implement a short-term voluntary officer system.

(3) To supplement the shortage of officers in peacetime and wartime, increase the number of special warrant officers.

(4) Abolish the donation system, making military service obligations equal regardless of wealth, and making the supplementation of reserve and reserve officer cadres appropriate and reasonable.

(5) Establish new training institutions for specialized non-commissioned officers (such as tank and chemical schools).

(6) Recruit young soldiers (under the age of 18) to serve as signalmen and airmen.

(7) Expand flight squadrons and tank squadrons (planning to expand to twice their current size).

(8) Establish new poison gas protection education institutions (modeled after the Soviet system, widespread throughout society, from children to women, all receive this type of education).

(9) Implement poison gas protection education in existing troops.

(10) Improve existing military police dogs and detection dogs.

The expenses for the above ten items are estimated at 12 million Japanese yen, and implementation began in January of this year.

As for the improvement of each division, given the current situation, on the surface, they still have to consider the Washington Treaty, so it is not convenient to increase the number of standing army divisions. Increasing the number of soldiers is also not permitted by the current national situation. Therefore, they are striving to enrich the content. They must increase airplanes, armored vehicles, tanks, direct-firing guns, and radio communication teams in each division. The goal is to be able to achieve the task of not being restricted by regional separation, especially the troops in the three northeastern provinces should be greatly expanded (to be able to control the Northeast Volunteer Army, and at the same time, to be able to invade Rehe and areas within Shanhaiguan at any time). In terms of combat materials, light and heavy machine guns, infantry artillery, grenade launchers, light howitzers, as well as various new equipment for poison gas protection, weather observation, and terrain observation, as well as medical supplies and veterinary supplies, are all being equipped more thoroughly and extensively. The total cost is approximately 9.29 million Japanese yen.

Increasing Troops to Manchuria

Regarding the invasion of North China, it is difficult for them to openly say they are attacking, nor can they say they are increasing troops to "Manchuria". Therefore, they only use the name of alternating stationed troops, transferring the 2nd Division, which has suffered too many casualties and has been guarding for too long, back, and replacing it with the 6th Division. According to the General Staff Headquarters' regulations, the duration of the division's stationing in "Manchuria" is from April 1933 to April 1934. However, in reality, the 36th Brigade of Kagoshima received mobilization orders at the end of November 1932 and departed in early December, and has now all arrived in the Liaoning and Jinzhou areas.

At the same time, the 1st Cavalry Brigade of Narashino suffered heavy casualties in the battle in northern Manchuria. Therefore, approximately 1,500 replacement soldiers and over a thousand military horses were transported from Tsuda Osamu (station). Over a thousand cavalry soldiers and over a thousand military horses were also transported from Utsunomiya (station). Other various weapons are being transported secretly, not allowing the general public to know (because the military transport is loaded onto the trains after 12:00 at night, but someone will always find out). The Kyushu area is smaller and mostly located by the sea, so it is easy to conceal. Currently, in addition to the military transport to Kyushu being incalculable, it is difficult to know the number of troops, wounded soldiers, and remains passing through Kashima, Ihi, and Mukatsu stations each time, but the number of transports is secretly recorded by workers at those stations as follows:

Troop Transport: 308 times

Wounded Soldier Transport: 98 times

Remains: 56 times

This is a small statistic from September of last year to November of this year. Of course, there are omissions in between, there will only be more, never less. Now that the 6th Division has arrived in Liaoning, it is feared that it is not just a rotation of troops, and there will inevitably be more alarming actions on the border areas of Rehe and Shanhaiguan. (December 31st)

Result of the Neijiang Conference

Yang Sen Proposes Equal Distribution of Benefits, Liu Xiang Opposes, Ends in Discord

Chongqing Correspondence: Since the retreat of Liu Wenhui's troops, Liu Xiang, Yang Sen, Tian Songyao, Deng Xihou, Liu Cunhou, etc., convened the Neijiang Conference, which officially opened on December 28th of last year and closed on New Year's Day of this year. The conference was nominally to plan for the aftermath and end the Sichuan War, but in reality, it was no different from a conference to divide the spoils of war. Since the deployment of the Liu and Yang armies, they have gained control of no less than forty counties from the 24th Army's defense area, and have incorporated no less than two divisions of the 24th Army's troops. However, those who contributed more received fewer benefits, and those who contributed less received more, which was very unfair. Therefore, the Neijiang Conference was initiated. Those who participated included Liu Xiang of the 20th Army, division commanders Pan Wenhua, Tang Shizun, Wang Zuanxu, and Fan Shaozeng, as well as Director of Political Affairs Gan Jixiong, Director of Finance Tang Dihzi, Yang Sen, army commander of the 20th Army, division commander Qiao Zhongquan, Tian Songyao, army commander of the 29th Army, division commander Wang Mingzhang, Ma Dezai representing Deng Xihou of the 28th Army, Liu Zhaoqian representing Liu Cunhou of the Sichuan-Shaanxi Border Defense Army, Li Jiayu of the New 6th Division, Luo Zezhou of the 23rd Division, and over fifty others. Yang Sen first proposed (1) Liu Xiang of the 21st Army should open up Yuwan, with all armies jointly stationing troops and establishing offices; (2) All armies should jointly station troops in Chengdu; (3) The 40 million yuan from the Jingyan salt tax should be divided equally among all armies; (4) The defense areas gained from the 24th Army should be divided among the Allied armies. Tian Songyao and Ma Dezai and Liu Zhaoqian, representatives of Deng Xihou, all expressed their agreement. Liu Xiang then said that while the 24th Army has not yet been completely eliminated, the above four proposals cannot be discussed at this time. We should all unite and completely eliminate Liu Wenhui before redistributing, to avoid misunderstandings at this time and giving the enemy an opportunity to take advantage. Tian Songyao agreed hesitantly. Li Jiayu and Luo Zezhou agreed. Yang Sen was disappointed. Thus, the much-publicized Neijiang Conference ended without result and adjourned. Yang returned to Zizhong, Tian Songyao returned to Chengdu, and Liu Xiang returned to Zigong, all mobilizing troops in preparation for war. Thus, the situation in Sichuan has become tense again. The reason why Liu Xiang refused to accept Yang Sen's proposal is that this Sichuan War was initiated by him, and he gained the most territory. Furthermore, he naturally does not want to share the Zigong salt tax with other armies. Opening up the cities of Yuwan is even more problematic. Liu Xiang's success today relies entirely on his exclusive control of Yuwan, which makes it easy to purchase and transport military supplies, and all transportation is convenient. If it is opened up, he will lose his monopoly. Currently, Liu Xiang is still attacking Jiading, Renshou, Jingyan, and Meishan with a large army. Li and Luo are also mobilizing. Tian Songyao, Yang Sen, and Deng Xihou's attitudes are ambiguous, but they are also mobilizing troops, and their intentions are not yet known. However, the Sichuan War will likely become even more chaotic. (January 5th)

Bandit Xu Plans to Flee to Eastern Sichuan and Enter Hubei

= Bao Chengqian has dispatched heavy troops to pursue and suppress =

= Tian Songyao telegraphs about the interception =

Hankou Correspondence: Xu He's remnant bandits fled from Shaanxi some time ago. Xu's bandits fled to the Suiding Tongjiang area of northern Sichuan, while He's bandits fled back to their old nest in Hefeng, western Hubei. Wherever they went, they slaughtered indiscriminately, especially Xu's bandits. Northern Sichuan is mountainous and complex, no less so than the border areas of Henan, Hubei, and Shaanxi. Xu's bandits are disturbing the area and treating it as a new base. Commander-in-Chief Chiang, based on intelligence, telegraphed the 29th Army of Sichuan, under Tian Songyao, to do their best to prevent them from entering. Tian sent the divisions of Li Weiru and Liu Hanxiong to jointly defend Tongjiang, Nanjiang, and Guangyuan with Liu Cunhou's Sichuan-Shaanxi Border Defense Army. In the end, the bandit forces were rampant and broke through. Tian telegraphed Chiang to report, saying, "According to a telegram from Commander Li Weiru, the vanguard of Xu's bandits, about 3,000 men, was completely repelled on the morning of the 31st of last month. However, the main force of the bandits continued to arrive, in great numbers. I personally supervised the battle in the Yangbai River and Yinggezui area, killing countless bandits. Our side suffered casualties, including battalion commander He and Yang, and over ten company and platoon commanders, and hundreds of soldiers. According to a transfer telegram from Regiment Commander Xue Yan of Nanjiang, relayed by Brigade Commander Wan Xuanqing, over two regiments of Red bandits have been discovered in the Dahekou area of Nanjiang. In addition to ordering Regiment Commander Xue to intercept and suppress them, I have also dispatched Battalion He stationed in Ba to assist. I have ordered Commander Liu Hanxiong of Guangyuan to lead his troops to Nanjiang as quickly as possible to join forces with Commander Li to suppress the bandits, and have also dispatched the Qin Brigade of Huang Zhengui's division from Mianyang to Guangyuan, and the Luo Brigade to Jiange, to assist in the suppression. I have also ordered the entire Luo Yanqiong Division to advance to Bazhong, under the unified command of the division commander, to coordinate with the central armies and the Shaanxi army, to complete your plan to annihilate the Red bandits in the short term." He Chengjun, who is in Shaanxi to supervise the suppression, upon learning of Xu's bandits fleeing south, immediately convened a military conference in Xi'an and decided to take advantage of the bandit's unsettled state to pursue and suppress them. He has dispatched Liu Maoen and Hu Zongnan's divisions from Shaanxi to Sichuan. As the bandits are planning to flee to eastern Sichuan and enter Hubei to join He's bandits in Hefeng, he has specifically dispatched Xiao Zhichu's division from Shaanxi via Ankang to northwestern Hubei to cut off their communication. Xiao's division mobilized on the 4th and will be able to concentrate at their destination within a few days. He will also convene Yang Hucheng, Sun Weiru, Feng Qinzhai, Hu Zongnan, Xiao Zhichu, and other generals in Xi'an again to hold a military conference to discuss a thorough elimination plan. He is scheduled to return to Hankou in a week. According to other sources, He still needs to stay in Shaanxi to preside. It is not yet determined when he will return to Hankou. Furthermore, Zhushan and Zhuxi counties in northern Hubei have long been occupied by bandits. Recently, the bandits have been defeated by Fan Shisheng's troops, and both counties have been recovered. In southern Henan, Hao Mengling's troops stationed in Luotian, eastern Hubei, have been dispatched to suppress the bandits. Hao has personally led the Wang and Liu brigades out of Tongluoguan, Qingtaiguan, and Songziguan, moving north. According to a telegram from Hao on the 5th, he has reached Wujia Store in Shangcheng County and will join the Henan army to search and suppress the remnant bandits to pacify the area. (January 5th)

The Headquarters for Suppressing Bandits Sends Personnel to Collect and Transport Special Goods from Northern Anhui

Bengbu Correspondence: In order to prohibit opium, the headquarters for suppressing bandits in the three provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui has dispatched special personnel to set up a collection and transportation office for special goods from northern Anhui in Bengbu. After the office was established, it has formulated the collection and transportation quotas for over twenty counties in northern Anhui, divided into five grades. Over a three-month period, each county ranges from 1,500 yuan to over 100,000 yuan. One collection and transportation officer is dispatched to each county, and over ten people have been appointed. Before leaving, they must first pay a security deposit, which is 3% of the quota. For example, if a county's three-month quota is 10,000 yuan, the collection and transportation officer must first pay a security deposit of 300 yuan. The important counties have mostly been appointed, and only Fuyang, Sixian, Chaoxian, and Lujiang counties have not yet been appointed. Most of those who have paid the security deposit have already left. Many of those who have been appointed but have not paid the deposit are still staying in Bengbu. The regulations for the collection and transportation of special goods in each county in northern Anhui are recorded below:

(Article 1) In order to comply with orders to collect and transport special goods from northern Anhui, this office will dispatch personnel to handle collection and transportation matters in various counties. (Article 2) The collection and transportation officer's term is limited to three months. Within the time limit, they must thoroughly clear out all special goods within the county, supervise the transportation to this office, and transfer them for destruction. The methods are as follows: (A) The procedures are divided into three periods: notification, purchase, and confiscation. (B) In the first period, all households with special goods are notified to report the amount within a time limit, obtain a verification certificate, and pay a monthly fee of 3 jiao. The collection and transportation officer should immediately fill out a report form and receipt. (C) In the second period, all households with special goods that have not reported or have reported falsely and are still hiding them beyond the time limit of the previous paragraph should first sell them at the price approved by the headquarters. (D) In the third period, if they still do not report and sell them during the purchase period, they will be treated as contraband and confiscated and punished after one day. (The time limit for reporting and the time limit for purchasing are determined by the collection and transportation officer and reported for record.) (Article 3) If the collection and transportation officer encounters any obstacles in handling matters, they may consult with the county government or public security bureau for assistance. (Article 4) From the date of arrival in each county, the collection and transportation officer should gradually report the reported situation of each household to this office and dispatch personnel to supervise and affix the verification certificate. (If households with verification certificates affixed according to regulations wish to transport the goods themselves, they may do so.) (Article 5) When transporting special goods, the collection and transportation officer should apply to this office for a shipping permit. (Article 6) If the collection and transportation officer finds any cases of private possession, private transportation, or private sale, or if they are reported by someone and verified, they should immediately submit the contraband to this office for review. If the quantity is within 100 liang, they may consult with the local county government or public security bureau to punish them according to the amount of the unpaid fee, and report the handling situation to this office for record. (Rules for rewarding informants will be formulated separately.) (Article 7) The amount of verification certificates that the collection and transportation officer receives for sale should be paid off in four installments within two months from the date of arrival in each county. One-quarter of the payment is due each installment. The first installment is due in 25 days, the second installment in 15 days, and the third and fourth installments are each due in 10 days. They must also pay a security deposit of 3% in advance and submit a recent four-and-a-half-inch half-length portrait and a guarantee from two reputable shops to this office for verification and record. (The security deposit, photo, and guarantee will be returned after the officer's duties have been reviewed.) (Article 8) The collection and transportation officer shall not reduce the quota or resign midway during the term of office in order to evade responsibility. Article 9 (The collection and transportation officer should supervise the affixing of the verification certificate according to regulations and shall not charge excessive fees.) (Article 10) The collection and transportation officer shall not collect beyond the scope of the area designated by this office. (Article 11) The collection and transportation officer shall report the collection situation to this office every five days for verification. (Article 12) If the collection and transportation officer fails to pay the installments due within five days, this office will dispatch personnel to collect them. If they still refuse to pay in full, the officer will be dismissed and punished. The guarantor will be held liable for compensation. (If there is a shortfall at the end of the purchase period, a fine of one times the amount may be imposed.) (Article 13) If the collection and transportation officer's performance exceeds the quota, they are allowed to withdraw 60% of the excess as a bonus. The best performers will be recommended for commendation. (Article 14) The collection and transportation officer will be issued a seal by this office as a token of good faith. It should be returned after the purchase period. (Article 15) If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, they may be amended at any time. (Article 16) These regulations will be implemented from the date they are approved by the headquarters for suppressing bandits in the three provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui. (January 5th)

Three Provinces of Hunan, Jiangxi, and Anhui Request the Levy of Import Duties on Foreign Rice

Intended to Relieve Grain Surplus in Various Regions

Anqing Correspondence: As foreign rice has been dumped in various provinces along the Yangtze River in recent years, causing rice sales in the provinces to stagnate and farmers and merchants to suffer, the Anhui provincial government has separately consulted the provincial governments of Hunan and Jiangxi, requesting that they consult the Ministry of Finance and promptly order the customs to increase import duties on foreign rice in order to resist it. The provincial governments of Hunan and Jiangxi have both replied in agreement. The original consultation from the Anhui provincial government is recorded below: "According to a report from Li Yunqi and others, the director of the Wuhu Grain Administration of this province, Annam rice has been imported from Shanghai and entered various provinces along the Yangtze River in large quantities, causing rice to stagnate in this province and unable to be transported out. We request a solution to this situation. The provinces along the Yangtze River have long been rice-producing areas. In years of average harvest, in addition to reserving enough food for the people for one year, the surplus has been transported out by tens of millions of dan per year. In addition, this year's harvest is bountiful and grain prices are low, and everyone is trying to sell to other ports to avoid low grain prices harming farmers. Now foreign rice is competing for sales inland. If we do not urgently resist it, not only will the rights and interests flow out and affect the economy, but also the grain surplus in various regions will cause farmers and merchants to suffer. This is truly harmful to the national economy and the people's livelihood. In view of this, this provincial government has immediately increased import duties on foreign rice in order to resist it. In addition to consulting the provincial government of Hunan (or Jiangxi), if you agree, please reply promptly so that we can draft a joint consultation and submit it. We hope to maintain public friendship." (January 7th)

The Jiaohai Customs Confiscates the Yongchang Ship

= The Ship was Carrying Japanese Sugar, Evading Taxes and Unloading Illegally =

= The Customs Discovered the Evasion and Confiscated and Punished the Ship =

Qingdao Correspondence: The Jiaohai customs has confiscated the Yongchang ship and made it public property because it evaded taxes and secretly transported Japanese sugar to Shijiusuo from Dalian for illegal unloading. It was discovered that the Yongchang ship belongs to the Changji Shipping Company in Shijiusuo. The company manager, He Ren'an, usually specializes in transporting Japanese goods from Dalian and other places. Since the customs canceled the Shijiusuo regular customs last year, He thought there was an opportunity to take advantage of. He colluded with the Japanese and jointly purchased three steamships from Japan to transport Japanese goods from Dalian and secretly unload them at Shijiusuo. The amount of evaded taxes is estimated to have reached over 600,000 yuan. This time, the Yongchang ship loaded 8,000 bags of Japanese sugar in Dalian. The captain of the ship, who is Japanese, declared the ship to Haizhou from Dalian. According to regulations, it should go directly to Haizhou and cannot call at another port. However, the ship secretly changed the logbook during the voyage and secretly went to Shijiusuo. After the ship arrived at Shijiusuo and secretly unloaded the Japanese sugar, the Japanese captain of the ship made an excuse and escaped. The first mate (Chinese) then sailed the ship to Haizhou. Unexpectedly, the matter was discovered by the customs, which telegraphed Haizhou. The ship was seized on the 14th of this month. At that time, the first mate and others knew that things were not going well and all fled without a trace, leaving only lower-level crew members who were not responsible. The company manager, He Ren'an, was panicked upon hearing the news. He secretly went to Shanghai on the 18th to ask the Japanese to find a way to intercede with the authorities, hoping to preserve the 8,000 bags of Japanese sugar, even if the ship was confiscated. It is heard that the customs has decided to confiscate the Yongchang ship. As for the tax-evaded Japanese sugar, in addition to paying the full amount of tax, it will also be punished twice as much to serve as a warning. The customs originally intended to sail the ship to Shanghai. After leaving Haizhou, the internal machinery of the ship suddenly malfunctioned, so the route was changed. It arrived in Qingdao yesterday (the 27th) and is temporarily docked at the Xiaogang pier for repairs before sailing to Shanghai to be handed over to the customs for inventory. Since this incident occurred, the Haizhou Customs has been paying close attention to such ships. The other ships of the Changji Shipping Company have only been sailing to Zhaozha and Shijiusuo in recent days and dare not go to Haizhou again. (December 28th)

Songjiang

Recent News on the Songxing Bank Failure Case

The Songjiang Bank failure case, after creditors petitioned the procuratorate, accusing [the bank] of fraud and other crimes, was ruled to be dismissed without prosecution. The creditors then applied for reconsideration. The procuratorate has now sent a letter to the liquidators, accountants Xi Yushu and Xia Sunhuan, requesting them to investigate and reply regarding the causes of the bank's failure and whether the defendants engaged in fraud, embezzlement, or collusion. Based on the review of the bank's account books, they are to determine the amount of bank funds embezzled by the bank manager and directors, the amount of fraudulent accounts, and provide a detailed list and expert opinion. The accountants replied, stating that the documents received by the liquidators were all submitted to the court by the former bank liquidation committee. These documents did not include crucial evidence such as vouchers, making it difficult to make assumptions. As of the liquidation, discrepancies found in the accounts include items listed as mortgage loans with no collateral, items listed as guaranteed loans with no guarantee, and accounts without real names or addresses, totaling over 300,000 yuan. This situation suggests embezzlement and fraud, for which the bank manager is undoubtedly to blame. As for the directors and supervisors, the liquidators cannot provide an assessment based solely on the account books (omission). If the responsible personnel of the bank were ordered to hand over the vouchers and bills, there would be a basis for the assessment. It is reported that the lawyers representing the bank's creditors are collecting relevant documents and drafting a report on the course of events and various evidence, and will send representatives to Beijing to petition [the government].

Suzhou

Robbery by Bandits on a Train

At approximately 6:10 PM on the seventh, on the slow train from Beijing to Shanghai, in a third and fourth class carriage, about five miles from Xu Guan, three bandits were discovered. They all spoke with a northern accent and were armed with small knives, robbing passengers. Four passengers were robbed in total. The bandits then disembarked midway and escaped. After the train arrived at Suzhou Station, Chen Chunyun, one of the robbed passengers, reported the incident to the station police, who immediately dispatched armed soldiers to apprehend the bandits.

Gao Ying's Wife, Liao, Released from Prison

Gao Liao, wife of Gao Ying, the former vice consul in San Francisco, was sentenced to two years imprisonment and a fine of 2,000 yuan after appealing to the High Court in a drug trafficking case. She was imprisoned in the Jiangsu Second Prison on Siqian Street in Suzhou. Since giving birth in prison in the spring of the previous year, her health has not recovered. Her husband, Gao Ying, was released after serving his sentence, but there has been no news of him for a long time. Now that Mrs. Gao's sentence has been served and the fine has been paid by her husband Gao Ying, Liao was released from prison on the fifth and has left Suzhou to return to her ancestral home in Guangdong for medical treatment.

Bank Employee Arrested After Embezzling Large Sum

Hu Fuxiang, an employee of the Bank of China in Hankou, was arrested in Suzhou after embezzling a large sum and fleeing with a prostitute. The prostitute, Zhang Suzhen, was also arrested in Shanghai. Xu, the manager of the Bank of China in Suzhou, requested the Public Security Bureau to send officers to Shanghai to bring Zhang Suzhen and others to Suzhou for handling by the Public Security Bureau. Yesterday, Wu, a clerk, interrogated Hu Fuxiang, who confessed that he had worked at the Bank of China since the eighteenth year and had embezzled 16,400 yuan. He met Zhang Suzhen in Hankou and had stolen 10,000 yuan in silver from the bank, which he gave to Zhang Suzhen and another prostitute, Yueying, in two installments for safekeeping. He claimed that after arriving in Suzhou, he had only 4,080 yuan left after paying off debts. After the interrogation, he was detained pending verification.

Clash Between Villagers and Refugees

Over a hundred refugees from Hunan arrived at Yinshan Town in rural Suzhou the other day, traveling on seven boats. After landing, they forcibly occupied a primary school and demanded money and rice from the villagers. The security corps sent a team to suppress them, provided them with six yuan for food, and escorted them out of the area. However, at 1:00 PM that afternoon, the refugees returned to Nanchangbang Village and demanded money and rice from a farmer named Jiang. They tied up Jiang's wife with rope and stole five or six shi of white rice. Some of them even fired guns. The villagers became enraged and clashed with them. When the police arrived, over a dozen refugees had been wounded by the villagers' flintlock guns. Six flintlock guns and eight villagers were seized and taken to the police station. The refugees were housed in a temple, and twenty-four wounded refugees were sent to Boxi Hospital for treatment. The county government and county security committee are now convening a meeting of the village chiefs and district security corps leaders to discuss a solution.

Jiading

Bullet Explodes, Injuring Tinsmith

On the afternoon of the fifth, Wang Jiao, the chief inspector of the County Public Security Bureau, instructed Rui Liansheng, a tinsmith at the Ye Hengchang tinsmith shop on West Street, to add tin to a high-explosive artillery shell to make a seal. Rui initially declined due to the danger, but Wang said that he had separated the warhead and the shell, and had poured out the original gunpowder, so there was no danger. Rui then worked according to Wang's instructions. Unexpectedly, when he applied a hot soldering iron to the warhead, it exploded violently. Apparently, Wang did not know that although the gunpowder in the shell had been removed, there was still explosive in the warhead. With a loud bang, shrapnel flew out, injuring Rui and other tinsmiths nearby, including Zhang Yongqing, Qiu Axue, and Xi A根, totaling four people. They were immediately sent to Jiading Hospital, where Dr. Geng Shiting provided treatment. Rui's left middle finger was fractured and dislocated, and his face, chest, arms, and other parts of his body were seriously injured. He fell unconscious after being admitted to the hospital. Zhang's injuries were also not minor. Rui is still in the hospital and his condition is not out of danger. The other three have been discharged.

Convict Escapes from Prison

Liu Shaolan, a native of Waigang, was imprisoned for drug offences. Last year, near the end of his sentence, he was found to be selling red pills in prison. The county government added six months to his sentence and imprisoned him in a solitary cell. Unexpectedly, the prisoner took advantage of the fact that it was difficult for others to see him in the solitary cell and secretly dug a tunnel, escaping at the beginning of the year. After he was discovered, police detectives apprehended him at the home of Liu's relatives in Shagangqiao. He has been sent back to the county for interrogation.

Military Officer Secretly Carries Large Quantity of Drug Pills

Yesterday afternoon, at the Liangxi Road, Merchants Steam Navigation Company wharf, under Gongyun Bridge in this county, when the Liyang-bound steamboat was about to set sail, Wei Jiaqi, Han Zian, and Tao Wenhua boarded the boat and inspected the luggage of a man in a yellow wool military uniform who appeared to be a military officer. The military officer resisted the inspection. Wei and others reported to Chen Zhenling, the seventh patrol officer of the Sixth Team of the Second District of the Provincial Water Police stationed at the wharf, who went to inspect. The military officer also resisted the water police inspection and went to the Gendarmerie Regiment Headquarters to report. Fearing that he would escape, Officer Chen followed him and arrested him, bringing him back to the wharf. Unexpectedly, the military officer's luggage had been taken away by Wei Jiaqi and others. Officer Chen then located Wei and others, who handed over two tins of "Fast Up" and "Fast Poison" pills, totaling two thousand pills. After strict questioning by Team Leader Shi, the military officer confessed his name as Zheng Yang, a native of Hubei, a graduate of the Central Military Academy. He said that he was traveling from Shanghai to Li阳 and had been entrusted by a friend in Shanghai to carry forty-four packets of "Fast Up" and "Fast Poison" pills, totaling eighty thousand pills, worth 1,120 yuan, hidden in his luggage. Understanding Life Insurance and Its Benefits

(The author of this article is a recognized writer on life insurance matters, having devoted over three decades to this industry. He began his career in London, serving in the life insurance actuarial department of Sun Life Assurance Co. of Canada. He then worked simultaneously in the actuarial department of Manufacturers Life Insurance Company. Within a few years, he and his colleagues founded Crown Life Insurance Co. in Toronto, where he served as a managing director. Later, he was hired by China Mutual Life Insurance Co. of Shanghai to reorganize the company, serving as a managing director. Subsequently, he resigned to organize China United Assurance Society, Ltd, a purely Chinese-owned company. It was inspired by the 1911 Revolution, taking the improvement of the national economy as its mission, and pioneering the Chinese life insurance industry. The author assisted in the organization, serving as manager and honorary director for over two decades).

Life Insurance by 郁赐 S.J. Hughes

It is difficult to define life insurance in just a few words without using complex scientific terminology. This vast and beneficial social organization is already well known in other countries and does not require further theoretical explanation. However, in China, this kind of public understanding and appreciation seems to be lacking. The total number of life insurance policies in the entire country is probably less than the monthly business of a single foreign company. Therefore, it seems permissible to occupy some space here for the readers' benefit.

Simply put, all kinds of life insurance policies can be considered a form of compensation. This compensation is to guarantee against significant losses by pre-paying a small fee. These losses may or may not occur within a specified period. Fire insurance and water insurance are more easily understood due to their more immediate needs. If the insured event occurs during the insured's lifetime, the insured can receive compensation. Hence, it is easier to popularize.

Slow Development in the Past

Life insurance, because the actual beneficiaries are those other than the insured himself, progresses slowly in public appreciation. Those who take out life insurance are not only thinking of their own happiness but also acting out of their natural love and considering those dependent on them. As for themselves, they only get the satisfaction of fulfilling their duties as a son, husband, or father, and the peace of mind that comes from being prepared. Life insurance prevents unexpected events from leaving dependents unprepared, and the examples of life insurance are also ways to encourage people to take out life insurance.

Originating Centuries Ago

The origin of life insurance dates back centuries. Friends would agree to pool money to provide relief to the surviving family members of those who died first. This is the beginning of the life insurance system. Outside of China, this system has become very popular worldwide and is an essential element for the well-being of society and the economy. What was once merely a private agreement among a small number of individuals has now become a specialized business. The value of the life of anyone capable of production, and the cost of insuring against unforeseen events, has been accurately statistically determined through the scientific application of actuarial rates and life expectancy.

Great Significance

Besides its own specialized science, the life insurance business requires the support of advanced mathematics, statistics, finance, economics, business management, medicine, and law. This article is only the first in a series on the general idea of life insurance. Therefore, we will not discuss the practical aspects of various applications. What is described here is only the great significance of life insurance for the happiness of individuals and society, and for the progress of the national economy. Although the idea of insurance is old, its adoption as a core enterprise of social organization is relatively recent. Its most recent public recognition came during the last World War. President Hoover of the United States once spoke about life insurance during the last election, saying that the last World War caused the loss of 40 million strong men in various countries, which deeply instilled the concept of the effectiveness of life insurance in people's minds. They not only deeply felt the relief provided by the life insurance business but also clearly understood that life should be insured early to prepare for unforeseen events. The deep-seated nature of this concept marked the last World War as the first time in the history of the life insurance business.

Amazing Progress

Since that time, life insurance, as the easiest, most reliable, and most economical way to restore a portion of financial losses to those who depend on a producer after his sudden death, has been more widely recognized and accepted by the public. In the recent fifteen to twenty years, life insurance has made amazing progress. If measured by the size of the population, North America, especially the United States and Canada, is the most prosperous. Even the recent impact of economic decline has not only failed to hinder its progress but has, on the contrary, promoted it. The economic decline in the United States was most severe in 1931, but the total amount of life insurance and the increase in assets that year also broke previous records. According to statistics at the end of last year, the total assets of life insurance companies in the United States, including the increase of $1,320,389,000 this year, totaled more than US$20,000,000,000.

China Can Adopt It

The evolution of humanity is endless, and the development of society is infinite. Life insurance has experienced amazing development due to the needs of evolution. This beneficial system, which is extremely developed in other countries, can certainly be adopted in China in order to seek the happiness of the people in terms of society and economy. We will discuss this in detail in another article. The author has been engaged in insurance for nearly forty years, and has personally experienced all aspects of the business. Therefore, what I say is not comparable to those who have no experience.

In summary, life insurance is one of the best ways for people to work together to improve human well-being. It makes wealth accessible to ordinary people and distributes it fairly, eliminating poverty. The huge sums of money gathered by life insurance companies are a material expression of various excellent human qualities, such as wisdom, thrift, and sacrifice. Are there those who want to replace the economic system that has developed over many years with social or communist doctrines? The national wealth represented by these insurance companies, that is, the huge sums of money saved by the working masses, is enough to encourage and reward the human conscience, and is a perfect answer for them. The world is changing day by day, and this unique system of self-help and cooperation, tested over a long period of time and adopted by people because of social needs, is now thriving.

The Meaning and Benefits of Life Insurance

— Chen Keqin

(1) Meaning

Life insurance is a method for many people to contribute a certain amount of money to prepare for compensating anyone among them for economic losses due to death, disability, or old age. From a social standpoint, life insurance is a strategy to accumulate funds to compensate for economic losses due to death, disability, etc. This kind of loss is transferred from individuals or a few people to be jointly borne by the public.

Generally speaking from an individual's perspective, life insurance is a reciprocal contract whereby the insured pays premiums, and when death or other specific events occur, the insurer compensates the insured or their beneficiary with a stipulated amount of money. The insurer can be an individual, an autonomous organization, a company, or the government. The beneficiary can be the family, business organization, or anyone closely related to the life of the insured (commonly known as the policyholder). This relationship is the insurable interest of the beneficiary in the insured.

(2) Benefits

The most important function of life insurance is to establish a personal life insurance estate to replace the value of life. In addition, life insurance also covers various other economic needs, which can be prepared for the following points:

(1) To repay debts after death. (2) To redeem mortgages.

(3) To guarantee children's education expenses. (4) To prepare large sums for donations.

(5) To prepare for family monthly income. (6) To prepare funds for sustenance in case of disability.

(7) To prepare for retirement and leisure gardens in old age.

(1) To repay debts after death.

Under today's economic circumstances, it is almost impossible for anyone, especially the head of the household, to pass away without outstanding debts. Such as electricity, fire, food and clothing, rent, medical expenses, etc. These accumulated arrears are indeed a burden on the family. However, a life insurance policy can provide funds to repay these debts.

(2) To redeem mortgages.

Loans secured by housing as collateral are debts that the family should first repay when the head of the household dies. Therefore, people with mortgage debts can take out life insurance equal to the mortgage amount in advance. When unexpected death comes, the debt can be repaid with the insurance money. In this way, the head of the household can guarantee that his wife and children will have a house to live in after his death, and can reunite and live the leisurely life they are accustomed to.

(3) Guarantee of children's education expenses

Higher education is becoming increasingly important in the country. The future happiness of children depends entirely on the training they receive in their youth. University education and even secondary education require financial backing. Therefore, parents should prepare a fund for their children's higher education before they pass away. This fund can be prepared through the parents' life insurance.

(4) Preparation of large sums for donations.

Endowments to charitable organizations or educational institutions often cannot be resolved quickly due to the complexity of inheritance lawsuits, the complexity of taxes, and the cumbersomeness of legal procedures. However, the recipient organizations often urgently need cash. Under today's circumstances, cash is much more useful to them than money that can only be received indefinitely in the future. Life insurance allows the donor to have the recipient receive cash immediately upon death.

(5) Preparation of family monthly income

Today, there is another type of policy that prepares the beneficiary to receive monthly income from the company within a considerable period of time. In this way, although the policyholder dies, his family still has living expenses. Most life insurance policies give descendants the right to receive money for several years. However, unfortunately, very few people use this method. After receiving a large sum of money, beneficiaries often waste it on various useless expenses due to lack of experience, or invest it in worthless businesses. Lifetime annuity policies guarantee that the policyholder's descendants can receive a fixed income on time. Therefore, large sums of money will not fall into the hands of inexperienced descendants, or be wasted or deceived into making useless investments. Even if it is not a lifetime annuity policy, a fixed-term annuity policy is enough to provide the family with living expenses until the children have received sufficient education to be self-reliant and have the surplus to provide for others.

(6) Preparation of funds for sustenance in case of disability

Most policies stipulate preferential terms that the policy remains valid if the policyholder becomes totally or partially disabled due to an accident. The content of this clause and the benefits that the policyholder can enjoy due to disability vary. However, generally speaking, there are the following three things:

(A) The premium during the period of disability does not need to be paid.

(B) The policyholder is paid ten units of currency (such as gold yuan, silver yuan, rupees, etc.) per month for every thousand units of currency (e.g. gold yuan, silver yuan, rupees) of the insured amount.

(C) The company pays the policyholder or beneficiary the face value when the contract expires, without deducting the amount of premiums not paid due to disability.

All of these are of great benefit to people who generally rely solely on personal work to earn income for living. Because disability makes them feel more difficult than death. According to the results of a survey, 38% of new life insurance policies in the United States have disability benefits. The amount of compensation that the company allows to pay out each year for the above reasons exceeds 220,000,000 units.

(7) Preparing a retreat garden for old age retirement

In American society, people have a very thorough understanding of the benefits of life insurance to families. However, they still regard the expenses for preparing for old age retirement with indifference. Recently, the importance of the annuity problem has been aroused by the investigation of the total number of old-age dependents in several provinces. Anyone should also consider their own life problems after their productive years have passed, after they have made sufficient preparations for their families. Life insurance can be used to prepare for the sustenance of the family when they depend on him for life. When the family can be independent, he can change the cash value on his policy into an annuity to prepare for his own old-age care.

Fortunately, our soldiers understand the righteousness deeply and resist bravely, giving the enemy a head-on blow in order to destroy the enemy. However, the enemy's strength is fierce and stubborn, and the war cannot but expand. The national situation is critical and in the balance. Our female compatriots account for half of the national population. The rise and fall of the country is everyone's responsibility. Our association was originally organized to unite female comrades from all over the country to provide relief to the compatriots in Northeast China who are in distress. In the future, the responsibility will be even greater. The Japanese invaders are brewing a great war and annexing the world. They have already mobilized the whole country. For the sake of our own defense and national salvation, shouldn't we also mobilize the whole country? We deeply hope that all our sisters in the country will rise up, each do their best, and do their best to work together to provide a solid backing for our soldiers and compatriots in the war zone. The situation is urgent and dangerous. We respectfully send a telegram to appeal." The China Women's Association for Relief of Northeast Compatriots, bow, Zhi Xue Dubi Talks: A reporter from Xinsheng News Agency met with Zhongwei Xue Dubi yesterday to ask for his opinion on the loss of Shanhaiguan. Xue said, "The Japanese invaders did not spend a single soldier or a single bullet to get the three northeastern provinces. Their progress is even more unscrupulous. It was expected long ago. However, we do not work hard ourselves and do not plan for self-salvation. We mistakenly rely on the League of Nations and then mistakenly hope for luck. We are sitting and waiting for death. It is extremely painful. Now that Shanhaiguan has been lost and North China is in danger, there is no other way but to fight desperately to seek survival from death. However, resisting Japan must be the central government's greatest and final determination to fight a protracted and deadly battle with the Japanese invaders with the entire strength of the country. Only then can it be of any use. Otherwise, it will be tense for a while, and people will forget it after the event. I am afraid that it will still be unavoidable to follow the old set of so-called long-term resistance or negotiation while resisting. The future is really unimaginable." The reporter also asked, "If the resistance to Japan is implemented, can the internal be united and united?" Xue said, "If the great plan of resisting Japan can be realized, then the trend will be unified, the spirit will be consistent, and anyone with a patriotic heart will definitely be happy to die for saving the country. There will never be any more problems internally. It can be said that the current situation is that national salvation cannot be achieved without resisting Japan, and unity cannot be achieved without resisting Japan. This is what I firmly believe."
