Sun Jinshun is indeed extraordinary and makes a name for himself unexpectedly. Youyou defeats Fashang.

Western Union First Group Victory

= Result: 3 to 1 =

= Sun Jinshun Scores Two Goals Alone =

The skills of a famous general are indeed extraordinary. With the effectiveness of the two great generals, Sun Jinshun and Huang Ruihua, they were indeed able to defeat the French Chamber of Commerce. On the Western Union First Group scoreboard, they have won once, adding two points. Since the formation of the team, they have been in a losing position in every match, except for two draws, avoiding a shutout. From now on, heroes from across the country will surely flock to join them. Sooner or later, Youyou (the team) can recapture the past glory of the Sanyu team. This all depends on the efforts of those in charge.

(Reputation is well-deserved) Sun’s fame is known to all, even women and children. With the announcement of his participation, five to six thousand Shanghai fans gathered, an unprecedented event for a Youyou match in recent years. Sun Jinshun is a famous "iron leg," his shots sharp, powerful, and magical. Since Li Huitang left Shanghai, we have not seen such amazing skill for a long time. Donghua's Li Yichen occasionally possesses it, but his movements are still not fast enough. Yesterday, Youyou won by three goals. The first goal was a gift from the opponent, actually created by Sun Hupei's efforts. For the second goal, in the sunlight and shadows, Sun’s iron leg kicked, and with a resounding "bang," the ball was already in the net, surprising the goalkeeper and delighting the spectators. For the last goal, he broke into the empty city alone and, with a sudden bang, the enemy's goal fell. From then on, Youyou’s victory was secured. His name is first on the list of merits.

(Full of vitality) Huang Ruihua, who has been a soldier for more than ten years, is once again seen by us on the playing field. The welcome he received is conceivable. His passing and receiving are still amazing, but his interceptions are somewhat diminished. According to rumors, Huang has been neglecting his training recently, and his skills are not yet fully honed. Given some time, he will surely return to his former self. In addition, the performance of the other nine players was also different from the past. Right-winger Chen Bogui made great contributions with Sun's guidance. The forward Ye Pumian and the inside back Qian Yaobin did their best in defense. Xi Qisheng is gradually improving. The overall situation was such that there were many surprising peaks in the first half, and the team suffered double the pressure from the opponent in the second half. Although they won, it was a nerve-wracking experience.

(Failure to reach the goal) The French Chamber of Commerce came with the determination to win, but faced with Sun and Huang, one inside and one outside, they were helpless and fell into a disadvantage. By the end of the game, the entire army advanced and attacked fiercely, and Youyou, which had the advantage, had to retreat to defend its territory and protect its land. Their Marseille had outstanding talent, and no one could approach him alone. Goalkeeper McNally, left-winger Foucault, and right-inside Fafan also had amazing skills. Therefore, there was always hope of recovering. For want of a final effort, they failed to complete their plan, failing to score due to a lack of shooting skill.

(Enemy Reverses) Before three o'clock, the stadium was full of fans, craning their necks and staring, waiting for the Iron Head and Iron Leg. Before long, a burst of applause, and two teams entered the field one after another. Youyou was on the south side, deploying its formation. The French team kicked off, and as soon as they started moving, Huang Ruihua rushed out from the center and passed it to his old partner, Sun Jinshun. Remy could not stop him, and Marseille did not dare to be careless, immediately intercepting the ball and sending it forward. Ye Jinmian took the lead, meeting the ball with his head before it landed, and Sun Hupei got it. He let the horse go wild in the west, dribbling straight to the baseline, and crossed it with all his might. Marseille saw that things were not going well and hurried to block the Iron Leg, but the ball crossed in front of the goal, and the forward, Garnier, panicked. The ball bounced off his thigh and into the net.

(Goalkeeper Shows Off) Now that Youyou had scored a goal, the forwards became more and more successful. Shen Bogui was as slippery as a freed rabbit. He received a long pass from Shi Jinsheng and went into the hinterland alone again. Sun Iron Leg caught up, and Shen passed it low to the center. Iron Leg shot hard, and McNally punched it out, but it was stepped on by Huang, who dribbled into the enemy's camp again. At a suitable spot, he shot at the goal, accurately and quickly. McNally jumped up and tipped it into a corner kick to escape danger.

(Iron Leg's Masterpiece) The French Chamber of Commerce was able to barely survive because

they launched another attack. Huang Ruihua's two fists could not beat four hands, causing the enemy to penetrate deep into the hinterland. Fortunately, the two generals, Qian and Wang, successfully rescued the situation. Liang Guanlian and Guan Congrong dealt with the situation calmly, and Youyou’s goal was kept safe. Shortly after, Sun launched another uprising in the west. Hu Youcheng secretly assisted him. Iron Leg strode forward, his spirit swallowing mountains and rivers, and reopened the attack. Xi Qiaosheng got the ball and dribbled a few steps, then turned and hooked it. Sun raised his Iron Leg, and with a "bang," the enemy's goal was broken again. The applause from all around was like thunder. It was Sun's masterpiece.

(Enemy Invades) After dozens more attacks, the silver whistle blew, temporarily calling for rest. Sun Iron Leg gave military instructions on the spot, and the athletes received their teachings. As the battle drums roared, the warhorses leaped again. The French Chamber of Commerce came with the ambition to win, but enjoyed a double shutout in the first half, which made them enraged. Marseille especially rounded his eyes, his expression menacing, and commanded his soldiers to launch a large-scale counterattack. Fafan and Bauschut charged left and right, shooting at the goal three times. Liang Guanlian calmly handled the situation, and there were no mistakes. Soon after, Colette was offside in the penalty area, and the ball was able to escape danger.

(Dragon Gate Falls) Remy's strange soldiers suddenly rose up, shouting and killing incessantly. Colette did not stop, and Huang Ruihua, full of courage, intercepted the ball and passed it forward. Bogui set fire in the west, but unfortunately, he was not successful in his campaign, and Garnier blocked his path. Bauschut made a comeback, connecting with Fafan and Jedden to launch an attack on three fronts. In an instant, Fafan let it go, and Jedden scored a goal in the midst of swords and shadows.

(Flying Cavalry Captures City) Since the score had become two to one, the French Chamber of Commerce was not satisfied and still thought of making peace under the city. The inner defense did not leave a single soldier, and all were sent out to besiege Youyou's goal no less than ten times. The two generals, Qian and Wang, met the attack separately. Huang Zhongjian filled in the gaps, his mind as careful as a hair. Twenty-five minutes of stormy waves turned into nothing in the blink of an eye. Huang Ruihua made a high pass, and Sun Jinshun was as fast as a galloping horse. The enemy's two backs were panting and could not catch up. McNally waited for the sentence with wide eyes. In a flash, the ball entered the French Chamber of Commerce's goal again. The fans on all sides praised and sighed. From then on, Youyou had nothing to fear, and victory was in their grasp. In the end, Youyou won three to one.

Two to One Wins Final

The Scott Tower Cup replay between Agaal and West Capture, the first game each tied with one goal, was held yesterday at the racecourse. As a result, Agaal won West Capture by two to one and won the right to the final.

▲West Capture scores one in the first half▲ Both sides fought fiercely, paying close attention to both offense and defense. The situation in the first half was average, without much difference. Commercial News

Financial Half-Day Gold Market Fluctuates Entirely With Large Traders

= Strength of Bulls and Bears is Equal =

= Continues to Rise by Two Taels and Four Qian =

(Summary) After the gold market rebounded the day before yesterday, people were optimistic overnight. Yesterday's overseas silver market did fall, with the London large bar shrinking by 0.1875. The British-American exchange rate did not change, while the American-British exchange rate fell by 0.040625. American silver was down by 0.0375, and the forward silver price also fell by more than 0.04. The bank's private telegram shrank by 0.005. The foreign exchange market opened slightly tight, and the gold price opened and immediately rose to 811.5 taels. After a slight rotation, it rose again, because Hengxing entrusted other companies to cover their short positions. However, because speculators Wu and Luo tried hard to sell, it went downstream even after rising to 13 taels, and the foreign exchange market also tended to ease. Yuan Maoyong (acting for Luo) and Qingfayong (acting for Wu) sold several times, so it fell to 0.062 taels. However, the Central Bank came to open up the spot market again, and Hengxing came on the scene and vigorously advanced more than 1,600 bars, and it rose again. At this time, the selling interest had faded, rising to 12 taels. People's mood was not good, because the American silver market was closed on the 8th, and its rise and fall could not be known. Those who profited sold off, and the price fell again, but Hengxing and others recklessly poured in at the 10-tael level, pulling the price up, and closed at 10.01 taels. In summary, there were no special changes in the half-day period. The entry and exit of large traders became the cause of the market price rise and fall. The Guangdong banks entered about 4,000 bars, Wu sold off about 1,000 bars, and Luo released about 2,000 or more. Here is a record of the market situation in half a day.

(Sketch) The opening price was 811.5 taels, a jump of 3.8 taels compared to the previous close. Dadecheng and items came to advance (items opened at 11.8 taels), and it rose to 2.8 taels. Qingfayong Yifeng Yonglai sold, and Pangen sold US dollars for February at 0.625, and then fell to 0.03. Zhifeng Yongheng Yu came on the scene and vigorously advanced, rising to 3 taels. However, the foreign exchange market was still loose. Yuan Maoyong Zhaofeng Chang sold, Sassoon sold US dollars for February at 0.6875, and it eased to 0.0625, falling to within 2 taels. However, the items continued to advance (at this time, Hengxing entrusted people to buy fiercely on the items), and even reached 3 taels. Fuyu Daxing Yonglai sold, and it went down again to within 1 tael. Hengyu Qing continued to deliver bars, rising to outside of 2 taels. After this, the sellers were active, and although the listing was small, the domestic market was hard. Sassoon sold again US exchange in January at 0.6875, and Fuyu Yifeng Yong took the opportunity to sell, thus breaking the 10-tael level and retreating to a half 0.08 tael. Dadecheng turned the bar, and the price was slightly fixed, but the sellers were still powerful. Qingfayong sold again, Sassoon cheaply sold US dollars for February, only doing 0.8125, falling to 0.062 taels. The Central Bank then opened the spot market several times, and people's mood was slightly stable. Hengxing came to advance, rising to outside 7 taels, but Yuan Maoyong happened to sell at this time, and the price was raised and suppressed between Hengxing and Yuan Maoyong. When Yuan Maoyong's selling energy was slightly killed, Hengxing vigorously purchased bars, and Yifeng and Yuan Xin Yong also advanced, thus breaking through the 10-tael mark. The Central Bank continued to absorb spot bids, and various spot numbers came to advance, and the foreign exchange market was also slightly better at 0.875. US dollars in March and bank dollars in February were also needed at 0.025. Returning to 12 taels, Daxing Yong and Items Hengyu repeatedly came to sell, while Hengxing bought from time to time at 10 taels inside and outside, so the price was raised and closed at 810 taels and 0.01 taels. People's mood looked down. The items were auctioned down by 0.01 qian, closing at 10 taels. The maximum in half a day was 813 taels, and the minimum was 0.062 taels, with a rise and fall of 6.8 taels. As a result, it continued to rise by 2.4 taels compared to the previous close.

(Opening the Spot Market) The Central Bank initially waited and watched, and after the gold price fell to 0.062 taels, it began to open the spot market, generally doing about five or six hundred bars within 10 taels, advanced by Hengxing Dadecheng Tongfeng Hengtai Kangrun and others.

Weekend Silver Dollar Market Routinely Weak

In the financial industry during the New Year, there is usually no development. Shanghai habits end the lunar calendar. It is impossible to expand the silver dollar business for a while. Foreign banks, especially the New Year, have few major transactions. On the Chinese bank side, the collections are also not strained. Although money houses sorting out closing procedures do not feel lonely, the abundant capital and surplus of silver are the root cause of the market's ills, let alone business operations. However, yesterday's collections were still weak. Even on weekends, it was not noticeably less. The swap market mostly went downstream.

(Foreign Li Gradually Decreases, Silver Swaps Remain Flat and Listless) The "foreign li" was weak yesterday morning, and the price plummeted when the market opened. The closing price was smaller by 0.001 than the previous day's afternoon market, at 0.07135. The afternoon market was slightly calmer, slightly higher than the early morning market by 0.000125, at 0.0713625. Based on the general trend, this market can get by during the lunar New Year. The "silver swap" in both the morning and afternoon markets was still 0.02, with a floating head plus water initially at 0.023, but then remained flat. The sluggishness of the silver capital situation is indescribable.

(Jiangguang Fell Early and Rose in the Afternoon, Copper Coins Continue to Shorten) The South minor foreign fell in the early morning, smaller by 0.005 than the previous day, calculated at 0.063, while the afternoon market rose again, calculated to have risen by 0.002, at 0.0632. There were 5,000 jiao of transactions made in the early morning market and 3,500 jiao in the afternoon market. The Guangdong minor foreign also fell early and rose in the afternoon, with the early morning market at 0.06175 and the afternoon market at 0.06185. As a result, it was slightly better by 0.0005 than the previous day's afternoon market. There were 65,000 jiao of transactions in the early morning market and 30,000 jiao in the afternoon market. The copper coin returned and shrank by 1,000 wen, to 391,000 wen. There were also few transactions, only more than 37,000 strings of wen.

(Foreign Exchange and Silver Markets Both Relaxed, Silver Collections Were Scattered) For "foreign loans," yesterday morning's exchange drafts only made 475,000 in the early market, and even less in the afternoon market, only 415,000. Banknotes were 35,000 in the early market and 45,000 in the afternoon market. Off-market banknotes were 60,000 in the early market and 75,000 in the afternoon market. Bank branch trades were 125,000 in the early market and 25,000 in the afternoon market. The interbank intermarket was 400,000 in the early market and 350,000 in the afternoon market. The receipt and payment of foreign accounts by each bank was 1,780,000, and the receipt and issuance of banknotes was 1,700,000. There was no news of customer route expenses, the money houses' foreign public single receipts and payments were 9,100,000, foreign remittance expenses receipts and payments were 2,220,000, swap foreign loan inflows and outflows were 2,440,000, small money houses' transactions were 800,000, and foreign mortgages were borrowed for 330,000. For "silver loans," yesterday's bank collections, although it was Saturday (the number was smaller), the scattered collections were still trivial and complicated. Foreign merchant receipts and payments for drafts were 1,770,000, Chinese merchant receipts and payments for drafts were 1,990,000, advances were 2,340,000, settlements were 3,000,000, special loans were 3,330,000, and various goods, remittances, taxes and miscellaneous expenses were collected and paid out by foreign merchants for 2,890,000 and by Chinese merchants for 4,340,000, mortgage transactions were 780,000, foreign merchants released 600,000 from warehouses, Chinese merchants entered 400,000 into warehouses, money houses' silver public single receipts and payments were 26,600,000, remittance expenses receipts and payments were 3,880,000, remittances to various routes receipts and payments were 550,000, and cash receipts were 230,000.

Deposit Interest Opened at Two Taels

At the regular meeting of the Money Industry Association the day before yesterday, it was resolved that the standard for deposit interest in December would still be calculated at the lowest rate of 0.0295 stipulated. According to the statistics of the silver swap in February, it was less than 0.01, which was the smallest statistical amount in the market, so it was resolved to use the stipulated low rate as the rate. As for overdue interest, it would be added according to the bottom rate of 0.045, so the highest overdue interest would still be no more than 0.1005.

Securities and Bond Prices Continue to Fall Sharply

Yesterday (the 7th), the transaction situation of various bonds on the Chinese Merchant Securities Exchange was as follows: the spot market was extremely clear, only opening up salt tax 19 Customs, and the futures market was still active. Important bonds came and went without being deserted, and the market sentiment remained weak. When it opened, it continued to fall across the board. Although there were no major changes afterwards, the trend remained very weak and there was no slight turning point. As a result, 15 Customs bonds for next month and 19 customs bonds for January each fell by more than 2 yuan, and others also fell by about 1.5 yuan. Only the Customs and Compilation bonds fell by only a few 0.06 or 0.07 yuan. The situation is still difficult to be optimistic, but the situation will no longer change, and there may be a temporary reaction. It is estimated that the futures trading in the morning was more than 4,550,000, and the after-market was 5,520,000, totaling 9,815,000 yuan. Spot trading totaled only 2,000 yuan.

American Cotton Focus Still on Rural Relief Bill

New York, January 6th telegram reports on the week's cotton market: Raw cotton prices this week recovered slightly due to purchases by industry participants and short covering, but southern sales also followed suit. The mid-week rally coincided with the revival of talk that Washington might pass an inflation plan, but there has been no substantial progress on this matter to date. The rural relief bill is the focus of attention for many, but it has had no significant impact on the cotton market here, as even if the bill is passed by the House, it will face even greater opposition in the Senate. Without a final disposition of this bill, people will be at a loss and uncertain, creating unrest and hindering the crystallization of opinions regarding the acreage of rice and cotton fields. According to the American Cotton Production News Agency, preliminary survey data indicates that planting intentions have not changed much. At the same time, reduced fertilizer application, signs of insect activity, and the decline in cotton farmers' enthusiasm all suggest that, under average weather conditions, yields per acre may decrease. (Zhabei) Yesterday, 40 to 50 boats arrived downriver. Sales of high-quality goods in stores were balanced. Secondary and inferior goods continued to be sold. Stockholders continued to buy mid-grade goods. The market for high-quality goods has stabilized. Secondary and inferior goods have slightly increased in price. Arrivals of rice are not strong. Another batch of Hunan Xian Yuan continues to arrive.

Foreign Rice and Raw Peanuts, Shanghai Stocks 330,000 Bags and 200,000 Bags

Yesterday, another batch of guest Xian rice continued to arrive from Hunan Province, including 1,700 bags of machine oil Jing and over 500 bags of machine Yuan. Dealers are mostly hoping for good prices. Because Minhua has not been selling well recently, they still dare not offer samples, relying on this to wait for opportunities. The Fujian gang has a strong purchasing interest, but because of the recent sale of river rice, the locking of guest Xian has turned dull. The quality of guest Yuan rice is better, and there is still social demand. However, because there are currently too many arrivals, shippers mostly want to sell quickly, so Yuan rice continues to soften. Yesterday, the Quanzhou gang bought 130 bags of newly arrived Hunan machine Yuan from the previous day at a price of 9 yuan and 4 jiao, which were high-quality long-grain rice. There are still 330,000 bags of foreign rice in Shanghai, mostly in the hands of British merchants Anli Xiangmao, etc. There is very little floating stock in the market. There is quite a demand on this street, but because the shippers are holding on to it, no sales have been made yet.

Yellow soybeans appetite is not strong, with a total of over a thousand bags traded. The market shape is difficult to determine for the time being. Flour Rises Sharply by Three Cents This Month

△Due to the sharp rise in foreign wheat and the shortage of flour in Tianjin△

Yesterday, the flour market was consistently strong in the morning. Foreign wheat rose by about 5 to 6 jiao. In addition, there is a current shortage of flour in Tianjin, and people are urgently purchasing. The spot goods of the troop transport ship have been completely purchased. Currently, the factory market for February is being bid for at two liang. Prices were seen to rise immediately at the opening. The Tianjin gang is still continuing to buy heavily in the near term. The forward market is being boosted by the rising price of foreign wheat. In the afternoon, the opening was still good. The market sentiment is unanimously looking for higher prices. The current price of foreign wheat is also more expensive than in previous years. No. 2 Kan wheat is being shouted for at four liang, although there have been no transactions, people's hearts are shocked by it. As a result, this month's price rose sharply by another three cents compared to the previous month. February and March rose by two and a half cents. April rose by four cents and two and a half li. May rose by three cents and seven and a half li. June rose by three and a half cents.

Wheat Futures Jump Eight or Nine Cents

Yesterday, the wheat futures market showed a consistent rising trend. Because there are very few spot goods for this month, there are only buyers and no sellers. Therefore, the market only has buyers raising prices, and those with actual goods are not releasing them for hedging. As a result, prices are rising unusually quickly. The price of foreign wheat has increased in the forward market. Australian wheat ordered before the new year was only three liang, five qian, five or six fen, but now it must be three liang and seven qian or more. Kan wheat has risen even faster, with No. 2 being raised to four liang, so people's hearts are also seen to be excited. Although there are few transactions, the price increase is also surprisingly high. Observing this situation, it is completely overshadowed by the impact of the war. How it will move forward is difficult to predict. As a result, this month rose by eight cents, February rose by five cents, March rose by seven cents, and April rose by nine cents. The rest are comparable. There are currently 300 bags, which have been purchased by the factories. The market is extremely firm.

Zhilu Goods, More Strong Than Weak, in North-South Goods

There was not much change in North-South goods during the holiday period. However, the price of golden needle vegetables has become cheap, the number of godown goods has tightened, and the intention to import is stronger. The price of ordinary wood ear fungus has also risen to fifty-two or three liang. Longkou vermicelli has been arriving frequently, but has recently rebounded slightly due to strong sales. Hunan lotus seeds have been rising in price due to the thinness of the stock and the firm holding of godown stocks. High-quality goods have reached fifty-eight liang, with a trend approaching sixty liang. Inferior goods range up to fifty-three liang. Locust rice is in short supply, and high-quality goods have risen to five liang and six or seven qian. Black wolfberries have also shown improvement. Longan godown prices are stable, and godown prices are slightly tight. Jinshan branch godown goods are firm and are unwilling to be sold cheaply. Lanzhu branches are flat, weak, and lack sales.

Silk and Tea Factories, Jingchou Sales Are Not Lonely

丨Shandong Da Er Wan Shou, More Than 500 Pieces Shipped to England丨

Yesterday, the silk market in foreign banks in this port still did not improve. Since the end of the year, there has been no new development in silk sales in European and American markets. Except for a few European banks in Shanghai that are making up for short-covering trades, actual sales are still in a wait-and-see mode. However, users of silk doors in inland areas have been increasing their appetite for yellow and white factory Jingchou, and transactions are not lonely.

This time, the British mail ship Sutton is exporting, and Xiangmao and others have another 570 pieces of Shandong Wan Shou being shipped to England.

Hardware, Overseas Tinplate Sees Another Price Increase

Tea Gang Buys Over a Thousand Pieces of Qing Lead

Since the outbreak of war in Yuguan, purchases of hardware by North Road guest gangs have greatly decreased. Business on Changjiang Road and Nanlu Road is also very depressed. The business of construction gangs and factories on this street is also small, so the market situation is quite quiet. However, tea godowns are very active in buying Qing lead, with a total of 1,300 to 1,400 pieces purchased (half of which are for delivery in February). The market price has increased considerably for a time and is currently at twelve liang and seven and a half qian, an increase of more than three or four qian from before. However, exchange rates have recently become expensive again, and it is feared that the standard will have to rise again. As for Hunan lead, arrivals are plentiful but sales are slightly lower, and the market remains normal. It is estimated to be at twelve liang.

After the Re-establishment of Sino-Russian Relations, the Vladivostok Gang Buys Large Quantities of Hardware

丨Tianjin Telegrams Stopped丨

Since the opening of customs, there has been no large business in hardware transactions. However, after the re-establishment of Sino-Russian relations, the Vladivostok gang is buying large quantities of metal products, totaling several thousand dan, including over seven hundred boxes of tinplate. The market price has been driven up by this, so it has reached twelve liang. There have also been several hundred dan of new lead wire, plain galvanized iron, and black iron sheet traded, with the prices of new lead wire and plain galvanized iron rising by two and a half qian. If there is no large influx of black iron sheet, there is also some business in white iron pipes, angle iron, new foreign silver dollars, etc., but not much. Due to Japanese troops invading the territory, the Tianjin and other gangs have stopped sending telegrams. As for the Yangtze River, Yantai, Fujian, and Guangdong gangs, there have also been no large transactions. In the past week, in addition to Qichang, Xintai Guogong and Xianghe godowns having slightly shipped new iron products, there is no news of arrivals from other agents.

Free Talk

Three Sleepless Nights

— Li Yun

I haven’t had a good night’s sleep for three consecutive nights, all thanks to my neighbors. The first night, after nine o’clock, they started playing mahjong. Besides the couple, there were two men’s voices, probably their friends. The tiles hitting the table sounded so crisp! It turned out they hadn’t even put a thin cloth on the table. Besides the sound of the tiles, there were occasional bursts of shouting. Indeed, playing mahjong is energizing. They were so full of vigor; the sound of the tiles on the table became louder and louder: crack, crack, smack! That’s what you call playing mahjong! It seemed like two of them were playing with all their might. If someone won a big hand, then the person sleeping next door was really out of luck. That burst of noise would wake you up even if you were sound asleep. This went on until two o’clock, and I could still hear someone resentfully shouting: "Four more rounds..."

The second night, late at night, the doorbell rang, and the husband came home. Not long after, his wife started arguing with him. The voice was angry and indistinct, but I could hear things like, "Shameless hussy, that dirty slut..." and the husband’s angry and malicious voice: "You're the slut! What business is it of yours? Humph..." Then, clang! I don’t know who smashed a teacup! No, maybe it was a rice bowl; who knows. Something heavy fell over, and it seemed like they were wrestling. Then it sounded like someone came to break them up. But after that, there were more curses and sobs, sometimes loud, sometimes soft. I don’t know how long it went on.

The third night, it seemed that the couple was not at home. Their son, who was studying at some university, had just come back from school. He was probably waiting for his parents because he turned on the phonograph. What was it? Some kind of recording. Oh, he was singing along! A woman’s voice! It really made my hair stand on end. From another room came the sound of a harmonium. That was his little sister; she was also inspired to sing. She was straining her throat to sing an outdated song called "Poor Qiu Xiang." They were each enjoying themselves, singing an out-of-tune ensemble. How lively! Shattering the neighbors' sweet dreams, what did that matter!

These three consecutive nights have given me so much unease and irritation.

Seize the Present!

— Xuan

Worldwide economic panic, bank failures, stock market crashes, factory shutdowns, tens of millions unemployed! Imperialists around the world desperately preparing for war, armories working day and night, deadly weapons piled up like mountains, newly invented poison gas numbering in the hundreds if not thousands! The world's "scholars" can no longer cover up the lies burned through, bitterly crying: civilization bankrupt!

Ah, ah, our world has reached an unprecedented era of transformation in human history!

Economic destruction across China, foreign goods like poisonous blood penetrating the veins of the countryside. Even in a so-called year of abundance, farmers have no food to eat! Rural unrest all over China, money running to safe havens, causing a deformed development of the urban economy, creating urban luxury, decadence, sin, rouge lips, jade legs, starry eyes, roulette, liquor, opium! All of China groaning and struggling under the iron heel of imperialism, deceived by Han traitors and national scum! China's "gentlemen" shake their heads and sigh: people's hearts are not as good as they used to be; the times are difficult.

Ah, ah, our China has also reached an unprecedented era of suffering in history! Yet it is also an era of transformation.

Dark and chaotic modern times! The fragile souls of petty citizens cannot bear this suffering of the "present"! They want to escape reality, they look up at the sky - the sky entrusted to God or the gods, they pin their hopes of consolation on the vague future! They look back - at the glorious past of the divine warriors, using it to deceive themselves!

The future, the future! This is expressed in the Kalachakra Tantra Assembly and in the ten or twenty years of "long-term resistance" enduring hardship with firm resolve!

The past, the past! This is expressed in the admiration for the "national hero" Yue Fei, the worship of Qi Jiguang, somewhere there are killers defending against Japanese pirates, somewhere there are platforms resisting Japanese pirates!... Our few literary giants count these "family treasures" backwards, unable to finish counting even after three days and three nights!

But what about the "present"?

The answer is silence, silence, a third silence!

But others are tightly seizing this "present," sharpening their swords and preparing their horses, invading and invading again!

Bah! Born in this era of worldwide transformation and China's suffering! Do not be obsessed with the past! Empty fantasies of the future! The past is already past; the future is only the future! Let us shout: -

Seize the Present!

Shen Congwen on Marriage

— Zhu Wen

Shen Congwen's novels are often praised for their mature writing and humorous language, but few know that this gentleman's letters are full of jokes and quite laughable. I remember in the summer of 1930, he was escaping the summer heat in Wusong and sent me a letter discussing marriage, saying:

"Because I am an old man myself, when I see young people with wives, even if they are not yet qualified to get married, I advise them to take the risk. (There's also the joke that I've been a matchmaker three times.) So I advise you to work hard at writing and also advise you to take the risk of getting married. Compared to women, career is nothing. People are only admirable when they are young, everything else is empty. But if you are young and spend your days in self-satisfaction, not knowing how to live well, then that young person is not worth mentioning. Love women, love friends, love life, do it well! Once you get older, it's all over. Women are only valuable when they are young. Letting young women grow old in the air is the sin of men."

Later, Ziyu and Luohong got married in Shanghai. Congwen happened to be in Qingdao and could not attend. On the auspicious day, I received a letter from Congwen and showed it to Hong. We recited it together. I told him about the previous letter, and we both smiled. Because he had encouraged marriage, he was now seeing Ziyu’s invitation. The letter said:

"Congratulations to you, the new groom, may you have a good life in the future. If you had sent me an invitation, I would have prepared a share of wedding wine. I really hope you will save my share, and I will drink it when I come to Shanghai in June to see your new home. The day of the wedding must be very lively. It's very different. I can’t see the demeanor of the groom. A couple of years ago, when Zhao Jingshen was the groom, it was very interesting. The fat man put on a formal suit rented from some shop. Many people were running around looking for a button or a belt. The groom just put his hand in a pocket on his waistband, wiping the sweat from his face, and kept tilting his head to one side, as if the stiff collar was tormenting his chin. After a while, firecrackers went off outside, darts were thrown, Western horns and Western drums were played, but I don't know who forced him to praise his wife with two sentences like writing poetry in the hall. He still remembered some moving words from his lotus leaf, and quoted a few sentences from Zhou Zuoren. Afterwards, it was naturally time to play music and drink. After seeing it once, I still think it's more vivid and interesting than his novels. Thinking of your wedding from that story must also be very happy.

Are you planning to live in Shanghai in the future or still go to Suzhou? If you two have the means, taking a trip to Beijing in this spring full of flowers would not be a meaningless trip. People say that in Qingdao during the honeymoon, the husband can be gentler, and the wife can be happier. You are such young and happy people. If you come to Qingdao, I am afraid you will be envied by the heavens and given rain, fog, and wind every day. This place in Qingdao knows that many young people get married in the spring and do not forget that Qingdao is very close to everywhere, and the place is quiet. Someone must be preparing to come and play, so the climate is always excellent. Only this spring, a large number of days have been almost terrible. Summer here is a good time to play. The various colors of the sea and the sky are indescribable, making people very peaceful.

I hope you will say hello to your wife for me. May God bless you and may you always have smiling faces in your life."

Serial Novel

The Crossroads of the Era and Love, Part 34

— Zhang Ziping

These were the first words Auntie Zhuo said after sitting down. Her smile seemed to carry a hint of cunning. Haiquan intuitively felt that this old woman was not easy to get close to. To put it bluntly, she was a woman whose intellect was too developed and not very understanding of human emotions.

After talking for a while, Haiquan learned that Zhuo Shuhua's elder brother, Shunxing, used to be a clerk in the ○○ bureau, but recently he was dismissed by the newly appointed bureau chief. However, he was reluctant to give up this job. He inquired and searched everywhere, and eventually found out that the new bureau chief was an old classmate of Ren Jinhua, and several people recommended by Ren Jinhua had been placed by the new bureau chief. Last week, he heard his sister mention that her classmate Lin Haiquan was Ren Jinhua's brother-in-law, so he asked his sister to pursue this path for him. "It's just a small job with thirty dollars a month. I think with a letter from Mr. Ren to the new bureau chief, I can definitely be reinstated."

Zhuo Shunxing explained earnestly.

"Mr. Lin, can you help us out?"

Zhuo Shuhua blushed and gave Haiquan a charming smile.

"I can see him on the fifth night..."

"Then that would be great."

Shunxing said with a smile, and it looked like he was about to applaud several times. Haiquan thought, it's just a small job with thirty dollars, and they're scrambling so hard for it. Tonight, he himself is like an important person. So, he became a little proud.

"Then please ask Mr. Lin to speak to Mr. Ren and ask him to write a letter to the new bureau chief, okay?"

Zhuo Shuhua wanted to push this matter onto Haiquan's shoulders. "But..."

He was still a little hesitant because he really wasn't sure.

"Please, Mr. Lin! For my sake!"

Zhuo Shuhua said, pointing to her face and smiling. Seeing her innocent expression, Haiquan couldn't bear to refuse. "Okay. I'll try to say something for you. I can't guarantee whether it will succeed or not."

"As long as Mr. Lin agrees, it's bound to succeed!"

Auntie Zhuo added more encouragement from the side.

Suddenly, the telephone rang, "Chilin, Chilin." Auntie Zhuo quickly spread her legs wide and walked over to answer the phone, holding the receiver to her ear. Haiquan saw her back view, which looked even more bloated and ugly.

"Okay... I know... That number... How can that work?... Tell him to go back!... Okay, okay... No, no. Okay, okay. That's what I mean..."

The old woman was listening to the phone while looking at Haiquan. Her expression seemed embarrassed, as if she was afraid of him overhearing something secret.

Auntie Zhuo put down the receiver and returned to sit at the square table.

"Who was that calling?"

Haiquan asked unconsciously.

"She was,..."

At that moment, Haiquan saw Shuhua quickly wink at her mother, and Auntie Zhuo changed her tone.

"Someone from the Moonlight Association was calling."

"It wasn't someone from Elder Sister calling!"

Amateur Musings

Reviewing the Past, Encouraging the Future

— Pu

(Last year, the three provinces were occupied; last year, Jinzhou fell; this year, Yuguan was lost; I don't know what will happen next year on this day?)

The alarm bell of "National Extinction! National Extinction!" has been ringing in China for more than fifty years, so most people hear the words "national extinction" as if it were a mantra to persuade people to do good deeds. Although the number of poor people in the country, the number of people without food, is increasing day by day, and the scope of the area where people are fighting for food - the bandit area - is expanding day by day, the entire political and social order is becoming more and more lax and chaotic. But most of the people who have more food to eat, who live in quieter places, especially the people in Shanghai, which is known as the ten-mile foreign concession, have a live-and-let-live mentality. "National extinction"? It's just talk; we ordinary people can't manage so much. People who have a better understanding of the international situation are even more eloquent in singing the grand truth that China will not perish under the balance of power in the international community. Therefore, the term "national extinction! national extinction!" has gradually diminished its serious meaning in the minds of Chinese people.

Like a bolt from the blue, on September 18th of the year before last, Shenyang City, Liaoning, was occupied by the Japanese army, and the key cities of the three provinces continued to be occupied. Following this, Jinzhou fell on January 2nd of last year, shocking the whole country. But in the midst of this shocking wave, apart from the compatriots in the three northeastern provinces who immediately felt the great disaster of national extinction descending, most people still felt that the League of Nations and the great powers would not stand idly by. As long as we argued on the basis of reason and at the same time did our best to help the volunteer army and strictly boycotted Japanese goods, we could achieve the final victory. To go even deeper, the important purpose of Japan's move was nothing more than protecting the rights it had already gained in the three northeastern provinces, or it had no ambition to occupy them for a long time, and so on. Unexpectedly, just when our whole country, from the government to the people, was panicking, hoping for luck and hesitating, the Japanese army, according to their well-thought-out plan, began to attempt to occupy the area around Shanghai within 24 hours. This shocked us, and all previous predictions were overturned. The danger of "national extinction," which we thought would not happen, immediately re-emerged in the minds of the Chinese people. Therefore, the brave resistance of the 19th Route Army won the support of the whole country. Especially the people living in Shanghai, which had always felt the safest, Zhabei, Jiangwan, Wusong, Zhenru, and Nanxiang all directly suffered huge sacrifices. Even Nanjing was threatened by shelling. The government moved the capital, and Hangzhou and Suzhou, which were considered paradises by the whole country, were visited several times by Japanese planes. Nanshi also spent more than thirty days in the fear of not knowing what the next day would bring. Even the people in the safest concession heard the sound of artillery every day and were terrified. At that time, we could see that the patriotic enthusiasm and the fear of national extinction of the people across the country had reached the highest level. Everyone felt the past carelessness and lack of preparation, especially the resentment against the government's lack of assertiveness and resistance - factional struggles, internal strife, selfishness, and corruption - which led to empty national defense and no way to resist the enemy. At the same time, everyone made a great determination, believing that the people and the government of the whole country should start from this day to correct their past mistakes and work together to do the work of national salvation by recuperating and training.

The 19th Route Army eventually retreated due to lack of support. The Japanese army, also due to the lesson of resistance, established the so-called Shanghai Agreement in understanding with the United Kingdom and France. Two weeks after the Shanghai battle stopped (March 14), the League of Nations investigation team came to China, putting on a show of visiting, investigating, and conducting on-the-spot inspections from Shanghai, Nanjing, Hankou, Tianjin, and Beijing all the way to the three northeastern provinces, and then returned to Beijing to write a report. On September 5, this once-sensational investigation team announced its departure from Shanghai. We observed the psychology of the whole country at that time, which was really wavering to the extreme. Before the Shanghai battle stopped, there were various resolutions to repent of the past and prepare for the future, but once the battle stopped, the investigation team arrived in Shanghai, and the agreement was signed, and traffic was restored, everyone's courage, determination, and fear disappeared with the restoration of the temporary peace, placing all their hopes on the investigation team. The people were like this, and the government was also like this. After the investigation team left the country, everyone hoped for the publication of the report, and after the report was published, they hoped that the League of Nations could strictly implement it. But during this period of hoping and relying on the League of Nations investigation team, what was the situation in our whole country? On the people's side, even the minimum boycott movement and the supply of the volunteer army outside the customs could not be thoroughly implemented, and active assistance was not provided. On the government's side, the central government concentrated all its efforts on suppressing bandits, and the internal affairs of the provinces were fighting with each other. After the investigation team left Shanghai, there was the Chen brothers' dispute in Guangdong, followed by the war between Han and Liu in Shandong, and then the suicide in Sichuan and the turmoil in Guizhou. When the war in Sichuan was at its fiercest, the League of Nations met, and all the resolutions gave us a "disappointment." The cry that the League of Nations was unreliable filled the whole country again, and at the same time, news of the Japanese army preparing to invade Rehe was heard from time to time. At this time, we do not know how the government was preparing, and the people were even more powerless. So, although we realized that the League of Nations was unreliable and knew that the Japanese army was planning to attack Rehe again, there was nothing we could do. Everyone had the mentality of waiting until after the New Year. Who knew that the Japanese soldiers did not pay much attention to the custom of celebrating the New Year and started attacking Yuguan on New Year's Day. The troops stationed there resisted for two days, and then retreated due to lack of support, so Yuguan fell on the afternoon of the third day at 2 p.m. Now Beijing and Tianjin are under great threat, and eight Japanese warships are stationed in Nanjing. The whole country is shaken again. The repentance and determination at the time of the Shanghai battle have been launched again, but what will we do?

Looking at the facts of the past, the shortcomings of our entire national character can be said to have been completely exposed. Our remedy now, which can be said to be the only way to save the country, is to have the following recognitions and resolutions from this day forward:

(1) If we do not make the greatest efforts and struggles, then in the near future, we will either become slaves of Japan or become international subjects. (2) It is always easier to remedy before the country is destroyed than to do it after the country is destroyed. (3) We must prepare in advance; it will be too late when the enemy is in front of us. (4) We should each start with ourselves, deeply repent, and strive for self-renewal. We should not blame others for following the old ways and living in peace. We should reflect on ourselves and strive to improve ourselves. We should first establish our personal will and then plan to gather like-minded people to fight together. We believe that as long as the majority of the country can do this, China will not be destroyed.

Problem Discussion

Suggestions for Resolving Labor-Management Disputes

— Ruan Guoyi

(Labor-management dispute issues)

In recent years, labor-management disputes have occurred almost every month. The reason is nothing more than the labor side not understanding the difficulties of the capital side, and the capital side not sympathizing with the suffering of the labor side, which has led to this unfortunate phenomenon. The labor side first makes demands, and then uses strikes as blackmail; the capital side first refuses to accept the conditions, and then uses dismissal as oppression, and ultimately both sides are injured and gain nothing. The capital side loses business income, and the labor side experiences mental pain. Even if one side wins, the feelings between labor and capital have been completely wiped out. Therefore, the capital side will increase the workload of the labor side to compensate for the extra expenses, and the labor side will never be willing to increase the efficiency of their work because of the victory. As a result, labor-management disputes start again. If this cycle continues for a long time, the capital side will inevitably stop starting businesses, the labor side will experience the fear of unemployment, and the entire society will become uneasy. Therefore, how to resolve labor-management disputes is a very important issue at present. As for the solution, it is necessary to combine the spirit of labor and capital into one body so that each has a personal stake in the matter. My suggestion is:

For example, if there is a factory with a capital of 10,000 shares, each share worth ten silver yuan, and there are 100 workers, each with a salary of twenty yuan; we should reserve 1,000 shares or 500 shares as worker benefit shares, and then deduct five percent of each worker's salary. To the extent possible, the capital side should provide a subsidy or "compassionate payment" equal to five percent of the salary and deposit it on their behalf each month. When it reaches ten yuan, a worker benefit share should be issued. This share should enjoy the same rights as other shares. In this way, a worker with a monthly salary of twenty yuan will have two shares of profit distribution in a year, and after ten years, he will have twenty shares of profit income. As the factory develops day by day, his profits will also increase day by day. Thinking of the increase in his own profits, he will definitely work hard to increase the efficiency of his work in order to ensure the factory's development and receive a large share of the dividends. This is just a small favor for the capital side, not only without loss, but also with unexpected progress; and on the labor side, in addition to gratitude, they will inevitably work even harder to maintain their interests because of their close relationship with the factory. If both labor and capital can always work together in this way, the result will be that not only will small capital become large capital, but workers will also become petty bourgeois elements. In this way, if there are labor-management disputes again, I will never believe it.

Furthermore, if a dismissed worker does not want to keep these shares, or needs the money for use, the capital side can also stipulate in advance that they can buy back his shares at 80% or 75% of their value. If a retired worker wants to keep his shares, he is free to do so. In short, as long as he has one share, the factory cannot cancel his status as a shareholder.

When the labor side has stable jobs, the capital side will have the spirit of starting businesses; when factories stand like forests, the unemployed masses will naturally gradually decrease, and the precarious Chinese industry and commerce may still have hope of being saved because of this!

The Life of the Industrial and Commercial World

The Sorrow of a Traveling Salesman

— Shi Sheng

(The Life of a Printing Employee)

"In the beginning, you're just 'following the salesman,' all you have to do is follow the traveling salesman around every day, all the time; then you've fulfilled your responsibility. Now you're a traveling salesman, you not only have to travel, but also bring in business. Bringing in business isn't enough, you also have to collect the money, otherwise, humph! The manager won't be happy with you." That was the lecture that Mr. Luo from our Shunxing Printing Shop gave me when I went from "following the salesman" to being a traveling salesman. At first, I was so scared I was sweating; this thing had the flavor of a pheasant soliciting customers. But at least the pheasant uses beautiful calling cards to solicit, enticing young gentlemen, making their hearts flutter. Who knows, they might follow her. The traveling salesman, no matter how eloquently you speak when trying to get business, saying things like "cheap and good, fast delivery," if the person listening isn't stupid, they'll definitely ask: "Then aren't you losing money?" "Building a reputation is important, making money is out of the question." Traveling salesmen all use this kind of "opening line," and the general affairs staff of banks and companies, they just prick up their ears and listen without caring, but on their mental hard drive, they have already etched the impression of several printing shops that offer 30% discounts on settlements, give gifts during the holidays, and where the traveling salesmen accompany them to drink and play mahjong. Those traveling salesmen don't need to quote prices, don't need to travel, the business comes on its own. Even if the manager of this bank or company opens a printing shop, the general affairs department will only give him a few remittance slips to print, just to save face. The bulk of the work is still sent to other printing shops. Unless, of course, the general affairs staff dies and is replaced by someone else. I'm a new traveling salesman, how could I know the secrets of this world? Sadly, I waste my leg strength every day, running back and forth, wasting my saliva, talking and talking, only to end up having several general affairs staff roll their eyes at me: "There's not much printing to be done here, don't come running here every day. If there's anything to print, we'll call you." This disguised expulsion order made me shudder, and I didn't dare stay any longer. I took a deep breath of cold air: "Goodbye, sir." When I retreated, the tea server would also glare at me a few times, scolding from afar: "Annoying!" Once, Manager Wang introduced me to Xingguo Bank to try to get business. The general affairs director, Mr. Sun, was an acquaintance of his. I went there and met Mr. Sun. He was really impressive,

Page 21

tall, with a long face, wearing a vest, and a very thick gold ring on his index finger, shining goldenly.

"Please sit, please sit, we're all acquaintances, we'll definitely take care of your business."

"I hope Mr. Sun will do his best to help."

"We're all family, no need to say so much. Please come by every morning!"

Following his instructions, I made sure to go there around nine o'clock every morning to discuss things. After three days of running around, he said to me: "The ledger design isn't ready yet, but when it is, we'll print at least a few hundred copies." A few times, he was out, and I had to sit on the sofa and wait. But, I, this traveling salesman with a hint of worker-like qualities, sitting in the magnificent bank office, was really causing the important gentlemen to look askance. Sure enough, a gentleman wearing a wool vest came to intervene: "Tea server, tell this traveling salesman to leave and come back after lunch."

"Yes! Yes!" I was very understanding, feeling small and insignificant, and didn't dare sit alongside the important gentlemen in the bank. So, without waiting for the tea server to drive me away, I took off running.

Back at the printing shop, lunch was already over, so I paid fourteen coppers and ordered a bowl of plain noodles. I had just finished eating when the phone rang: "Mr. Shi, Mr. Sun has asked you to come over." It was the tea server's voice, so I went again. When I met the tea server, he said: "Mr. Sun left just a moment ago, you came right after him, wait a while." I had already learned my lesson once, so I didn't dare sit, and stood waiting for a long time before Mr. Sun hurriedly came back. His butt had just touched the leather chair when he stood up again and ran outside, catching a glimpse of me, smiling and nodding: "Sorry, too busy today, come tomorrow!"

He finally took pity on me and took out two ledgers, saying: "Print two copies just like these, we need them urgently." I took the printing job back, and the next morning, the phone was ringing like a string of pearls: "What's going on! The ledgers haven't been delivered yet, if they're not here soon, we don't want them anymore... Printing so slowly, and you still want to get business!"

At the end of the month, Mr. Sun finally completed a twenty-dollar transaction. I sent an invoice to collect the money, and he tapped and tapped on the abacus: "Two eights are sixteen, pay sixteen dollars."

"The transaction isn't much, please pay the full amount."

"No, the price is too high, the paper is too thin, and the delivery is too slow, how can I not deduct anything?"

Three bills and one silver dollar, I had to accept them. I finally wrote a receipt. Coincidentally, Xingli Printing Shop also sent a receipt, which Mr. Sun quickly put away, but I had already seen a total amount of "Received seven hundred and eighty silver dollars."

I went back and handed the collected payment to the accountant, and Manager Wang said: "What's going on! This little amount, and you still gave a discount? The ledgers are only worth two dollars each, tell me, where does the paper, labor, ink, and expenses come from? We printed so little, and you still gave an 80% discount, we're practically losing money and about to close down! Mr. Shi, take less of these kinds of transactions." He then took out a spreadsheet, "This month, we lost five hundred dollars, please put in some effort next time, and hurry up and collect a few more debts."

Two days later, Mr. Luo suggested to me: "Mr. Sun from Xingguo Bank, you have to give him some kickbacks, otherwise, all of his business will go to Xingli." So this time when I went, I pulled Mr. Sun aside and quietly said: "Mr. Sun, I'll do whatever you say."

"Nonsense, nonsense, don't say that, Mr. Shi, you're underestimating me." He said sternly, as if declaring his personality was supremely pure, "There really isn't much to print, if there is, wouldn't I give it to you?"

"Mr. Sun, six hundred ledgers, four hundred invoices, have been delivered, please issue a receipt." The traveling salesman from Xingli Printing Shop shouted loudly, interrupting our conversation. Mr. Sun stood up, blushing.

I feel that my talent for traveling salesmanship is too poor, but at the same time, Manager Wang only knows how to exploit the workers, which greatly reduces the workers' efficiency. Often, printing jobs with a one-week deadline take ten and a half days to be delivered. Customers are furious, and the phones are filled with scolding voices like creditors demanding payment. But the machines still hum slowly like old cows during the day, only roaring at night, because there's extra pay for night work. Often, the workers set the wrong type, the proofreader doesn't see it, and when it's printed wrong, the customers return it. The manager says: "Traveling salesman, what were you doing when you received the sample?" Several general affairs staff members, when they see me, also say coldly: "Your products aren't refined, and the delivery is slow, what are you traveling around for, you should close down and go home." Poor traveling salesman – me – in the noise of the machines, I have already judged my future fate. Every time I come back, before entering the door, I always focus and listen to the machines. If they're roaring, my courage immediately grows and I enter happily. If, unfortunately, there's no sound at all, my heart immediately feels like a band of hair is tightly tied around it, and I'm afraid to cross the threshold.

The market is becoming increasingly depressed, and Shunxing's business is gradually declining. The machines sit quietly on the ground, silent all day. The workers are all shirtless, hiding under the windows, secretly playing chess. Several employees are waving palm leaf fans, wandering back and forth in the accounting room. Manager Wang is lying on the sofa, drinking soda, loudly scolding: "Traveling salesman, what are you doing for twenty dollars a month?" At this moment, I just came running back from outside, my clothes soaking wet as if I had just been pulled out of the water, large beads of sweat falling from my face to the ground. I take a breath, preparing to step over the threshold, and when I hear the scolding, I quickly turn around, tears welling up in my eyes, and step onto my path of life, step by step, under the scorching summer sun, on the fiery asphalt road!

From Trademark Disputes to the Decline of Industry

— Tian Fang

Recently, the Family Chemical Industry and the Huanan Chemical Industry have been engaged in a trademark dispute [details in the newspaper]. Both sides have been running large advertisements, each presenting their own strong arguments. In today's immature industrial sector, this is indeed a very serious issue, worthy of discussion. It should be stated that the reporter has no relationship with either party and wishes to explore the underlying causes of this dispute from the perspective of an observer, as well as the obstacles to promoting domestic goods, hoping for readers' corrections.

The cause of this matter is that Huanan Company uses the image of Ms. Hu Die as the trademark for its toothpaste, and the Family Industry believes that Huanan Company intends to confuse it with the company's "Invincible" trademark, and has requested the Trademark Bureau to revoke the registration of the trademark. But Huanan Company did not give up, but ran large advertisements, causing the Labor Bureau to issue a statement that it would "handle the matter according to the law and would never act based on sentiment." The future is unknown, the process is like this.

Here, we judge from the documents and reasons provided by both parties, and cannot help but say that Huanan Company is suspected of "innuendo." Because the use of trademarks with similar or identical sounds for similar items is prohibited by law. And "Hu Die" and "Invincible" - apart from phonetics experts, there is no distinction in ordinary people's mouths, and it also violates the prohibition of applying to similar items. Therefore, in terms of morality and law, Huanan Company cannot avoid considerable responsibility. But the reporter is not a judge, so I don't want to make a final judgment on the right and wrong of the two parties, but want to explore the motives and results of this dispute from the perspective of social psychology.

I believe that "innuendo" and "counterfeit" are no different from theft, and are a major reason for the decline of the domestic goods industry. The basis for this behavior is rooted in the national character of luck and laziness. The earth has no east or west, species have no black or white, human intelligence is equal, why don't we create something new? We must know that taking chances is just an act of viewing oneself as incompetent, but our society is filled with this atmosphere. All scissors sellers are Zhang Xiaoquan, all sauce meat sellers are Lu Gaojian, they don't think about creating their own style, and always want to seize what's already there. However, once a great reputation is overused, it is not enough to gain people's trust, this is really the most foolish and pitiful thing. And under these circumstances, how can the future of domestic industry have a flourishing atmosphere? Originally, competition in the same industry is an upward phenomenon, but it must follow the proper path, and compete on the essence, not on the name. Because "name is the reality of reality," if the reality is achieved, the name will follow. The general customer is not completely stupid, and although they can be confused by the name for a while, in the long run, they must rely on the substance. From the facts, before "Invincible" toothpaste was invented, Japanese diamond toothpaste had an annual sales volume of about five million yuan in our country's market. But now Japanese goods have disappeared, and many rights and interests have been recovered every year. I express my highest respect to Mr. Chen Xujun [although I don't know Mr. Chen]. I think it is worth emulating.

Promoting domestic goods and revitalizing industry are indeed the most important tasks of today. Because now, what we use every day, from a toothpick and a match, to clothes and utensils, are mostly imported goods, leakage is overflowing, which is really regrettable. There are many ways to reserve the labor of the industrial sector, and merchants are making profits, but they must put people's livelihood and the country first. If you turn your guns around and use the policy of self-cannibalization to compete with foreign industries, consumers in the third-party position will be happy to sponsor them. The success of "Invincible" toothpaste is a precedent. In the future, everyone will become an old brand, wouldn't everyone be "Invincible", so why fight with each other now, just to increase the joke? As the saying goes, "the goods sell for copper coins," we know that value is definitely not on a sign, so why should I show weakness? If you want your business to flourish, you only need to return to yourself. Those who have the heart to take chances, please reflect on it!

The main purpose of this text is to hope that people engaged in industry will abandon the mentality of taking chances and compete with others in terms of substance. Because customers are not completely deceivable, and there must be a way to make money.

Special Article

Scientific Personnel Management

— Geng You

Personnel disposition is the most important and most difficult issue to resolve in factory management. In fact, the so-called personnel management is entirely based on the psychological reform of both labor and management, sincere cooperation, fair treatment, not burying their individuality, following the trend of labor, and giving them appropriate work. If personnel management can achieve satisfactory results, then the initial goal of scientific management can be said to have been achieved; in other words, the first step in implementing scientific management is to achieve suitable personnel management, because if labor and management cannot be harmonious, then how can we expect the development of their business?

The location of factories is often based on the convenience of raw material supply and commodity sales, so remote areas with inconvenient transportation are not suitable for the establishment of factories. Conversely, the aggregation point of wheel ports and railways is the most prosperous area for commercial factories. People from all over the world live together, and their origins are different. Therefore, the temperament and habits of laborers are different. It is really not easy to melt them into one furnace.

Humans are the most complex and unstandardized animals. Due to environmental, natural, and other factors, the following differences arise:

(1) Physiological (physical) differences: differences in strength, weakness, height, shortness, fatness, thinness, etc.

(2) Mental differences: differences in talent, habits, hobbies, etc.

(3) Educational differences: differences in the level of education.

(4) Family relationship differences: family joys and sorrows are different.

(5) Ancestral differences: inheritance can be rich or scarce; leaving a good name or a bad name to descendants.

(6) Environmental differences: differences in origin, career, and starting point.

(7) Social situation differences: customs and human relations vary from place to place.

The differences between people are not just the above. Factory affairs cannot be done by one or two people. Large organizations often have tens of thousands of workers. Not only are their personalities different and their origins different, but their diligence, skill, and clumsiness are also different. Therefore, how to make management effective and workers happy to work is a major issue to be explored.

Humans are rational animals. The more suppressed, the more violent the reaction. Therefore, those who do things voluntarily perform better than those who are forced. Personnel management should apply the above principles and set up a personnel department to handle it. The outline of its duties is as follows:

(1) The employment or promotion of employees must be suitable for both talent and affairs.

(2) Analyze the nature of the work and the degree of difficulty to determine appropriate remuneration.

(3) The formulation of work standards should be used as a criterion for awards or training.

(4) Research on wage levels.

(5) Labor welfare, health, and safety issues.

(6) Encourage employees, such as implementing awards and other incentives.

(7) Train employees to increase work efficiency, and guide and assist their progress.

The scope of ordinary management is approximately as above. If we further study the situation of each worker, then the only thing left is employee investigation. The points that should be paid attention to in employee investigation are as follows:

(1) Each person's education level and experience.

(2) Each person's duties and work performance.

(3) The individual's feelings about the matter, whether there is any dissatisfaction.

(4) The individual's family situation and economic situation.

When implementing the investigation, it is best to be as detailed as possible, because laborers cannot approach the capital party on weekdays, and all their sufferings cannot be leaked. The authorities should use the investigation time to solve this huge problem. In particular, we must pay attention to whether they are interested in their duties, because engaging in any work, wherever the interest lies, will definitely get twelve points of good results, otherwise there will be no hope of improvement!

What needs to be closely watched is the managers themselves. If the managers can have a spirit of great impartiality and guide patiently; have a quick mind and distinguish right from wrong; have an accurate understanding of each person's work diligence; reward, comfort, and train them; and ensure that most laborers are happy to work, then scientific personnel management is almost achieved.

Self Occupational Introduction

Mr. Bao for Rent

— Bao Zhichun

[Forty Dollars per Month]

Q: Why do you want to rent yourself out?

A: Because I have no living expenses.

Q: Is forty dollars enough for your monthly expenses?

A: There is only a mother and a wife in the family, and forty dollars a month is indeed enough to cover expenses.

Q: What's your name?

A: My surname is Bao, and my name is Zhichun.

Q: Where are you from?

A: Qilin Town, Wuxing County, Zhejiang Province.

Q: Where do you live now?

A: No. 25, Lane 812, Xinzha Road, Shanghai.

Q: How old are you this year?

A: Twenty-two years old.

Q: What are your abilities?

A: I have strength, a loyal service heart, I can write, I can calculate, I can endure hardship, I can listen, I can see, I can speak, and I can serve for up to fourteen or sixteen hours a day.

Q: Where did you work before?

A: I used to work at the Nantong Dasheng Factory.

Q: Can you go out?

A: I can travel far and not bring my family. And I can never go home.

Q: Do you have a guarantor?

A: I have a loyal shop guarantor.

Clerk Correspondence

Recognizing a Thief as a Father, Caught in a Dilemma

Editor: I am a senior elementary school graduate. Two years ago, I dropped out of school to go into business because my father's business failed. But good things never come in pairs, and misfortunes never come alone. My boss is the public enemy of our people, the little Japanese. The day before yesterday, I decided to resign to implement the non-cooperation policy. But when I think back: if I resign, where will I go? Shanghai has no relatives or friends and cannot survive. Then go back to my hometown? My parents, who cannot take care of themselves, cannot afford to increase their burden. But if I don't resign, how can my conscience be at peace living this life of recognizing a thief as a father? Editor, I am really in great difficulty! Please advise me!

Wu Xinguo, December 31st

Editor's Note: Anyone who reads Master Wu's letter will sympathize with him, but "the non-cooperation policy is what any of our people should be willing to die to implement!!" Therefore, it is advocated that Master Wu should still resign. As for the problems after resigning, with two hands, as long as you are willing to endure hardship, it is not difficult to solve personal life. You must know that breaking stones and doing odd jobs is much better than the life of recognizing a thief as a father!! Besides, Master Wu has this ambition, and even if no one appreciates him for a while, someone will eventually promote him; he will not really go to break stones and do odd jobs. Finally, the editor hopes that those in society with power will help him to achieve his ambition. If you want to correspond with Master Wu, please ask the Amateur Weekly Society of the Library to forward it.
